## Sponsorships
> [![Digital Ocean](https://avelino.run/sponsors/do_logo_horizontal_blue-210.png)](https://m.do.co/c/bd3b723c0a36?utm_medium=opensource&utm_source=awesome-go)

**We have no monthly cost**_, but we have employees **working hard** to maintain the Awesome Go, with money raised we can repay the effort of each person involved! All billing and distribution will be open to the entire community._

A curated list of awesome Go frameworks, libraries and software. Inspired by [awesome-python](https://github.com/vinta/awesome-python).

### Contributing

Please take a quick gander at the [contribution guidelines](https://github.com/avelino/awesome-go/blob/master/CONTRIBUTING.md) first. Thanks to all [contributors](https://github.com/avelino/awesome-go/graphs/contributors); you rock!

#### *If you see a package or project here that is no longer maintained or is not a good fit, please submit a pull request to improve this file. Thank you!*

## Audio and Music

*Libraries for manipulating audio.*

* [flac](https://github.com/mewkiz/flac) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mewkiz/flac.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mewkiz/flac.svg) - Native Go FLAC encoder/decoder with support for FLAC streams.
* [gaad](https://github.com/Comcast/gaad) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Comcast/gaad.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Comcast/gaad.svg) - Native Go AAC bitstream parser.
* [GoAudio](https://github.com/DylanMeeus/GoAudio) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DylanMeeus/GoAudio.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DylanMeeus/GoAudio.svg) - Native Go Audio Processing Library.
* [gosamplerate](https://github.com/dh1tw/gosamplerate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dh1tw/gosamplerate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dh1tw/gosamplerate.svg) - libsamplerate bindings for go.
* [id3v2](https://github.com/bogem/id3v2) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bogem/id3v2.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bogem/id3v2.svg) - ID3 decoding and encoding library for Go.
* [malgo](https://github.com/gen2brain/malgo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gen2brain/malgo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gen2brain/malgo.svg) - Mini audio library.
* [minimp3](https://github.com/tosone/minimp3) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tosone/minimp3.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tosone/minimp3.svg) - Lightweight MP3 decoder library.
* [mix](https://github.com/go-mix/mix) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-mix/mix.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-mix/mix.svg) - Sequence-based Go-native audio mixer for music apps.
* [music-theory](https://github.com/go-music-theory/music-theory) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-music-theory/music-theory.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-music-theory/music-theory.svg) - Music theory models in Go.
* [Oto](https://github.com/hajimehoshi/oto) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hajimehoshi/oto.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hajimehoshi/oto.svg) - A low-level library to play sound on multiple platforms.
* [PortAudio](https://github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gordonklaus/portaudio.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gordonklaus/portaudio.svg) - Go bindings for the PortAudio audio I/O library.
* [portmidi](https://github.com/rakyll/portmidi) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rakyll/portmidi.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rakyll/portmidi.svg) - Go bindings for PortMidi.
* [vorbis](https://github.com/mccoyst/vorbis) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mccoyst/vorbis.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mccoyst/vorbis.svg) - "Native" Go Vorbis decoder (uses CGO, but has no dependencies).

**[⬆ back to top](#contents)**

## Authentication and OAuth

*Libraries for implementing authentications schemes.*

* [authboss](https://github.com/volatiletech/authboss) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/volatiletech/authboss.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/volatiletech/authboss.svg) - Modular authentication system for the web. It tries to remove as much boilerplate and "hard things" as possible so that each time you start a new web project in Go, you can plug it in, configure, and start building your app without having to build an authentication system each time.
* [branca](https://github.com/hako/branca) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hako/branca.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hako/branca.svg) - Golang implementation of Branca Tokens.
* [casbin](https://github.com/hsluoyz/casbin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hsluoyz/casbin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hsluoyz/casbin.svg) - Authorization library that supports access control models like ACL, RBAC, ABAC.
* [cookiestxt](https://github.com/mengzhuo/cookiestxt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mengzhuo/cookiestxt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mengzhuo/cookiestxt.svg) - provides parser of cookies.txt file format.
* [go-email-normalizer](https://github.com/dimuska139/go-email-normalizer) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dimuska139/go-email-normalizer.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dimuska139/go-email-normalizer.svg) - Golang library for providing a canonical representation of email address.
* [go-guardian](https://github.com/shaj13/go-guardian) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shaj13/go-guardian.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shaj13/go-guardian.svg) - Go-Guardian is a golang library that provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to create powerful modern API and web authentication that supports LDAP, Basic, Bearer token and Certificate based authentication.
* [go-jose](https://github.com/square/go-jose) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/square/go-jose.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/square/go-jose.svg) - Fairly complete implementation of the JOSE working group's JSON Web Token, JSON Web Signatures, and JSON Web Encryption specs.
* [go-oauth2-server](https://github.com/RichardKnop/go-oauth2-server) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RichardKnop/go-oauth2-server.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RichardKnop/go-oauth2-server.svg) - Standalone, specification-compliant,  OAuth2 server written in Golang.
* [gologin](https://github.com/dghubble/gologin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dghubble/gologin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dghubble/gologin.svg) - chainable handlers for login with OAuth1 and OAuth2 authentication providers.
* [gorbac](https://github.com/mikespook/gorbac) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mikespook/gorbac.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mikespook/gorbac.svg) - provides a lightweight role-based access control (RBAC) implementation in Golang.
* [goth](https://github.com/markbates/goth) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/markbates/goth.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/markbates/goth.svg) - provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to use OAuth and OAuth2. Handles multiple providers out of the box.
* [httpauth](https://github.com/goji/httpauth) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/goji/httpauth.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/goji/httpauth.svg) - HTTP Authentication middleware.
* [jeff](https://github.com/abraithwaite/jeff) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abraithwaite/jeff.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abraithwaite/jeff.svg) - Simple, flexible, secure and idiomatic web session management with pluggable backends.
* [jwt](https://github.com/robbert229/jwt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robbert229/jwt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robbert229/jwt.svg) - Clean and easy to use implementation of JSON Web Tokens (JWT).
* [jwt](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/jwt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pascaldekloe/jwt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pascaldekloe/jwt.svg) - Lightweight JSON Web Token (JWT) library.
* [jwt](https://github.com/cristalhq/jwt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cristalhq/jwt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cristalhq/jwt.svg) - Safe, simple and fast JSON Web Tokens for Go.
* [jwt-auth](https://github.com/adam-hanna/jwt-auth) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adam-hanna/jwt-auth.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adam-hanna/jwt-auth.svg) - JWT middleware for Golang http servers with many configuration options.
* [loginsrv](https://github.com/tarent/loginsrv) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tarent/loginsrv.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tarent/loginsrv.svg) - JWT login microservice with plugable backends such as OAuth2 (Github), htpasswd, osiam.
* [oauth2](https://github.com/golang/oauth2) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/oauth2.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/oauth2.svg) - Successor of goauth2. Generic OAuth 2.0 package that comes with JWT, Google APIs, Compute Engine and App Engine support.
* [osin](https://github.com/openshift/osin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openshift/osin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/openshift/osin.svg) - Golang OAuth2 server library.
* [otpgen](https://github.com/grijul/otpgen) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/grijul/otpgen.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/grijul/otpgen.svg) - Library to generate TOTP/HOTP codes.
* [otpgo](https://github.com/jltorresm/otpgo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jltorresm/otpgo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jltorresm/otpgo.svg) - Time-Based One-Time Password (TOTP) and HMAC-Based One-Time Password (HOTP) library for Go.
* [paseto](https://github.com/o1egl/paseto) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/o1egl/paseto.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/o1egl/paseto.svg) - Golang implementation of Platform-Agnostic Security Tokens (PASETO).
* [permissions2](https://github.com/xyproto/permissions2) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xyproto/permissions2.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xyproto/permissions2.svg) - Library for keeping track of users, login states and permissions. Uses secure cookies and bcrypt.
* [rbac](https://github.com/zpatrick/rbac) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zpatrick/rbac.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zpatrick/rbac.svg) - Minimalistic RBAC package for Go applications.
* [scope](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/scope) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SonicRoshan/scope.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SonicRoshan/scope.svg) - Easily Manage OAuth2 Scopes In Go.
* [scs](https://github.com/alexedwards/scs) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexedwards/scs.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexedwards/scs.svg) - Session Manager for HTTP servers.
* [securecookie](https://github.com/chmike/securecookie) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chmike/securecookie.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chmike/securecookie.svg) - Efficient secure cookie encoding/decoding.
* [session](https://github.com/icza/session) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/icza/session.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/icza/session.svg) - Go session management for web servers (including support for Google App Engine - GAE).
* [sessiongate-go](https://github.com/f0rmiga/sessiongate-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/f0rmiga/sessiongate-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/f0rmiga/sessiongate-go.svg) - Go session management using the SessionGate Redis module.
* [sessions](https://github.com/adam-hanna/sessions) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adam-hanna/sessions.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adam-hanna/sessions.svg) - Dead simple, highly performant, highly customizable sessions service for go http servers.
* [sessionup](https://github.com/swithek/sessionup) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/swithek/sessionup.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/swithek/sessionup.svg) - Simple, yet effective HTTP session management and identification package.
* [sjwt](https://github.com/brianvoe/sjwt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/brianvoe/sjwt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/brianvoe/sjwt.svg) - Simple jwt generator and parser.

**[⬆ back to top](#contents)**

## Blockchain

*Tools for building blockchains.*

* [cosmos-sdk](https://github.com/cosmos/cosmos-sdk) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cosmos/cosmos-sdk.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cosmos/cosmos-sdk.svg) - A Framework for Building Public Blockchains in the Cosmos Ecosystem.
* [go-ethereum](https://github.com/ethereum/go-ethereum) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ethereum/go-ethereum.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ethereum/go-ethereum.svg) - Official Go implementation of the Ethereum protocol.
* [gossamer](https://github.com/ChainSafe/gossamer) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChainSafe/gossamer.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChainSafe/gossamer.svg) - A Go implementation of the Polkadot Host
* [tendermint](https://github.com/tendermint/tendermint) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tendermint/tendermint.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tendermint/tendermint.svg) - High-performance middleware for transforming a state machine written in any programming language into a Byzantine Fault Tolerant replicated state machine using the Tendermint consensus and blockchain protocols.

**[⬆ back to top](#contents)**

## Bot Building

*Libraries for building and working with bots.*

* [echotron](https://github.com/NicoNex/echotron) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NicoNex/echotron.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NicoNex/echotron.svg) - Concurrent library for Telegram Bots written in pure Go.
* [ephemeral-roles](https://github.com/ewohltman/ephemeral-roles) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ewohltman/ephemeral-roles.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ewohltman/ephemeral-roles.svg) - A Discord bot for managing ephemeral roles based upon voice channel member presence.
* [go-chat-bot](https://github.com/go-chat-bot/bot) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-chat-bot/bot.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-chat-bot/bot.svg) - IRC, Slack & Telegram bot written in Go.
* [go-joe](https://joe-bot.net) - A general-purpose bot library inspired by Hubot but written in Go.
* [go-sarah](https://github.com/oklahomer/go-sarah) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oklahomer/go-sarah.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oklahomer/go-sarah.svg) - Framework to build bot for desired chat services including LINE, Slack, Gitter and more.
* [go-tgbot](https://github.com/olebedev/go-tgbot) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olebedev/go-tgbot.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olebedev/go-tgbot.svg) - Pure Golang Telegram Bot API wrapper, generated from swagger file, session-based router and middleware.
* [go-twitch-irc](https://github.com/gempir/go-twitch-irc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gempir/go-twitch-irc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gempir/go-twitch-irc.svg) - Library to write bots for twitch.tv chat
* [Golang CryptoTrading Bot](https://github.com/saniales/golang-crypto-trading-bot) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/saniales/golang-crypto-trading-bot.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/saniales/golang-crypto-trading-bot.svg) - A golang implementation of a console-based trading bot for cryptocurrency exchanges.
* [govkbot](https://github.com/nikepan/govkbot) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikepan/govkbot.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikepan/govkbot.svg) - Simple Go [VK](https://vk.com) bot library.
* [hanu](https://github.com/sbstjn/hanu) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sbstjn/hanu.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sbstjn/hanu.svg) - Framework for writing Slack bots.
* [Kelp](https://github.com/stellar/kelp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stellar/kelp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stellar/kelp.svg) - official trading and market-making bot for the [Stellar](https://www.stellar.org/) DEX. Works out-of-the-box, written in Golang, compatible with centralized exchanges and custom trading strategies.
* [margelet](https://github.com/zhulik/margelet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zhulik/margelet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zhulik/margelet.svg) - Framework for building Telegram bots.
* [micha](https://github.com/onrik/micha) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onrik/micha.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onrik/micha.svg) - Go Library for Telegram bot api.
* [olivia](https://github.com/olivia-ai/olivia) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olivia-ai/olivia.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olivia-ai/olivia.svg) - A chatbot built with an artificial neural network.
* [slack-bot](https://github.com/innogames/slack-bot) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/innogames/slack-bot.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/innogames/slack-bot.svg) - Ready to use Slack Bot for lazy developers: Custom commands, Jenkins, Jira, Bitbucket, Github...
* [slacker](https://github.com/shomali11/slacker) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shomali11/slacker.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shomali11/slacker.svg) - Easy to use framework to create Slack bots.
* [slackscot](https://github.com/alexandre-normand/slackscot) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexandre-normand/slackscot.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexandre-normand/slackscot.svg) - Another framework for building Slack bots.

* [config](https://github.com/olebedev/config) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olebedev/config.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olebedev/config.svg) - JSON or YAML configuration wrapper with environment variables and flags parsing.
* [configuration](https://github.com/BoRuDar/configuration) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BoRuDar/configuration.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BoRuDar/configuration.svg) - Library for initializing configuration structs from env variables, files, flags and 'default' tag.
* [configure](https://github.com/paked/configure) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paked/configure.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paked/configure.svg) - Provides configuration through multiple sources, including JSON, flags and environment variables.
* [configuro](https://github.com/sherifabdlnaby/configuro) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sherifabdlnaby/configuro.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sherifabdlnaby/configuro.svg) - opinionated configuration loading & validation framework from ENV and Files focused towards 12-Factor compliant applications.
* [confita](https://github.com/heetch/confita) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/heetch/confita.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/heetch/confita.svg) - Load configuration in cascade from multiple backends into a struct.
* [conflate](https://github.com/the4thamigo-uk/conflate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/the4thamigo-uk/conflate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/the4thamigo-uk/conflate.svg) - Library/tool to merge multiple JSON/YAML/TOML files from arbitrary URLs, validation against a JSON schema, and application of default values defined in the schema.
* [env](https://github.com/caarlos0/env) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/caarlos0/env.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/caarlos0/env.svg) - Parse environment variables to Go structs (with defaults).
* [envcfg](https://github.com/tomazk/envcfg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomazk/envcfg.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomazk/envcfg.svg) - Un-marshaling environment variables to Go structs.
* [envconf](https://github.com/ian-kent/envconf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ian-kent/envconf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ian-kent/envconf.svg) - Configuration from environment.
* [envconfig](https://github.com/vrischmann/envconfig) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vrischmann/envconfig.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vrischmann/envconfig.svg) - Read your configuration from environment variables.
* [envh](https://github.com/antham/envh) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antham/envh.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antham/envh.svg) - Helpers to manage environment variables.
* [fig](https://github.com/kkyr/fig) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kkyr/fig.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kkyr/fig.svg) - Tiny library for reading configuration from a file and from environment variables (with validation & defaults).
* [gcfg](https://github.com/go-gcfg/gcfg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gcfg/gcfg.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gcfg/gcfg.svg) - read INI-style configuration files into Go structs; supports user-defined types and subsections.
* [genv](https://github.com/sakirsensoy/genv) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sakirsensoy/genv.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sakirsensoy/genv.svg) - Read environment variables easily with dotenv support.

It supports reading the configuration from environment variables, config files and command line parameters.
* [go-ini](https://github.com/subpop/go-ini) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subpop/go-ini.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subpop/go-ini.svg) - A Go package that marshals and unmarshals INI-files.

Keep you config structs along with the code they configure and delegate parsing to submodules without sacrificing full config serialization.

* [goset](https://github.com/zoumo/goset) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zoumo/goset.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zoumo/goset.svg) - A useful Set collection implementation for Go.

* [gostl](https://github.com/liyue201/gostl) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/liyue201/gostl.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/liyue201/gostl.svg) - Data structure and algorithm library for go, designed to provide functions similar to C++ STL.
* [gota](https://github.com/kniren/gota) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kniren/gota.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kniren/gota.svg) - Implementation of dataframes, series, and data wrangling methods for Go.
* [goterator](https://github.com/yaa110/goterator) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yaa110/goterator.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yaa110/goterator.svg) - Iterator implementation to provide map and reduce functionalities.
* [hide](https://github.com/emvi/hide) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emvi/hide.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emvi/hide.svg) - ID type with marshalling to/from hash to prevent sending IDs to clients.
* [hilbert](https://github.com/google/hilbert) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/hilbert.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/hilbert.svg) - Go package for mapping values to and from space-filling curves, such as Hilbert and Peano curves.
* [hyperloglog](https://github.com/axiomhq/hyperloglog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/axiomhq/hyperloglog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/axiomhq/hyperloglog.svg) - HyperLogLog implementation with Sparse, LogLog-Beta bias correction and TailCut space reduction.
* [iter](https://github.com/disksing/iter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/disksing/iter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/disksing/iter.svg) - Go implementation of C++ STL iterators and algorithms.
* [levenshtein](https://github.com/agext/levenshtein) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agext/levenshtein.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agext/levenshtein.svg) - Levenshtein distance and similarity metrics with customizable edit costs and Winkler-like bonus for common prefix.
* [levenshtein](https://github.com/agnivade/levenshtein) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agnivade/levenshtein.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agnivade/levenshtein.svg) - Implementation to calculate levenshtein distance in Go.
* [merkle](https://github.com/bobg/merkle) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bobg/merkle.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bobg/merkle.svg) - Space-efficient computation of Merkle root hashes and inclusion proofs.
* [merkletree](https://github.com/cbergoon/merkletree) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cbergoon/merkletree.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cbergoon/merkletree.svg) - Implementation of a merkle tree providing an efficient and secure verification of the contents of data structures.
* [mspm](https://github.com/BlackRabbitt/mspm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BlackRabbitt/mspm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/BlackRabbitt/mspm.svg) - Multi-String Pattern Matching Algorithm for information retrieval.
* [nan](https://github.com/kak-tus/nan) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kak-tus/nan.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kak-tus/nan.svg) - Zero allocation Nullable structures in one library with handy conversion functions, marshallers and unmarshallers.
* [null](https://github.com/emvi/null) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emvi/null.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emvi/null.svg) - Nullable Go types that can be marshalled/unmarshalled to/from JSON.
* [ordered-concurrently](https://github.com/tejzpr/ordered-concurrently) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tejzpr/ordered-concurrently.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tejzpr/ordered-concurrently.svg) - Go module that processes work concurrently and returns output in a channel in the order of input.
* [parapipe](https://github.com/nazar256/parapipe) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nazar256/parapipe.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nazar256/parapipe.svg) - FIFO Pipeline which parallels execution on each stage while maintaining the order of messages and results.

* [ring](https://github.com/TheTannerRyan/ring) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TheTannerRyan/ring.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TheTannerRyan/ring.svg) - Go implementation of a high performance, thread safe bloom filter.

## Database

*Databases implemented in Go.*

* [badger](https://github.com/dgraph-io/badger) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dgraph-io/badger.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dgraph-io/badger.svg) - Fast key-value store in Go.
* [bbolt](https://github.com/etcd-io/bbolt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/etcd-io/bbolt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/etcd-io/bbolt.svg) - An embedded key/value database for Go.
* [bcache](https://github.com/iwanbk/bcache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iwanbk/bcache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/iwanbk/bcache.svg) - Eventually consistent distributed in-memory  cache Go library.
* [BigCache](https://github.com/allegro/bigcache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/allegro/bigcache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/allegro/bigcache.svg) - Efficient key/value cache for gigabytes of data.
* [Bitcask](https://git.mills.io/prologic/bitcask) - Bitcask is an embeddable, persistent and fast key-value (KV) database written in pure Go with predictable read/write performance, low latency and high throughput thanks to the bitcask on-disk layout (LSM+WAL).
* [buntdb](https://github.com/tidwall/buntdb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tidwall/buntdb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tidwall/buntdb.svg) - Fast, embeddable, in-memory key/value database for Go with custom indexing and spatial support.
* [cache](https://github.com/akyoto/cache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/akyoto/cache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/akyoto/cache.svg) - In-memory key:value store with expiration time, 0 dependencies, <100 LoC, 100% coverage.
* [cache2go](https://github.com/muesli/cache2go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muesli/cache2go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muesli/cache2go.svg) - In-memory key:value cache which supports automatic invalidation based on timeouts.
* [clusteredBigCache](https://github.com/oaStuff/clusteredBigCache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oaStuff/clusteredBigCache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oaStuff/clusteredBigCache.svg) - BigCache with clustering support and individual item expiration.
* [cockroach](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cockroachdb/cockroach.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cockroachdb/cockroach.svg) - Scalable, Geo-Replicated, Transactional Datastore.
* [Coffer](https://github.com/claygod/coffer) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/claygod/coffer.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/claygod/coffer.svg) - Simple ACID key-value database that supports transactions.
* [column](https://github.com/kelindar/column) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kelindar/column.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kelindar/column.svg) - High-performance, columnar, embeddable in-memory store with bitmap indexing and transactions.
* [couchcache](https://github.com/codingsince1985/couchcache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codingsince1985/couchcache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codingsince1985/couchcache.svg) - RESTful caching micro-service backed by Couchbase server.
* [CovenantSQL](https://github.com/CovenantSQL/CovenantSQL) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CovenantSQL/CovenantSQL.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CovenantSQL/CovenantSQL.svg) - CovenantSQL is a SQL database on blockchain.
* [Databunker](https://github.com/paranoidguy/databunker) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paranoidguy/databunker.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/paranoidguy/databunker.svg) - Personally identifiable information (PII) storage service built to comply with GDPR and CCPA.
* [dgraph](https://github.com/dgraph-io/dgraph) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dgraph-io/dgraph.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dgraph-io/dgraph.svg) - Scalable, Distributed, Low Latency, High Throughput Graph Database.
* [diskv](https://github.com/peterbourgon/diskv) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/peterbourgon/diskv.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/peterbourgon/diskv.svg) - Home-grown disk-backed key-value store.
* [dtm](https://github.com/yedf/dtm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yedf/dtm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yedf/dtm.svg) - A distributed transaction manager. Support XA, TCC, SAGA, Reliable Messages.
* [eliasdb](https://github.com/krotik/eliasdb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krotik/eliasdb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krotik/eliasdb.svg) - Dependency-free, transactional graph database with REST API, phrase search and SQL-like query language.
* [fastcache](https://github.com/VictoriaMetrics/fastcache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VictoriaMetrics/fastcache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VictoriaMetrics/fastcache.svg) - fast thread-safe inmemory cache for big number of entries. Minimizes GC overhead.
* [GCache](https://github.com/bluele/gcache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bluele/gcache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bluele/gcache.svg) - Cache library with support for expirable Cache, LFU, LRU and ARC.
* [go-cache](https://github.com/pmylund/go-cache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pmylund/go-cache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pmylund/go-cache.svg) - In-memory key:value store/cache (similar to Memcached) library for Go, suitable for single-machine applications.

* [groupcache](https://github.com/golang/groupcache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/groupcache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/groupcache.svg) - Groupcache is a caching and cache-filling library, intended as a replacement for memcached in many cases.
* [hare](https://github.com/jameycribbs/hare) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jameycribbs/hare.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jameycribbs/hare.svg) - A simple database management system that stores each table as a text file of line-delimited JSON.
* [immudb](https://github.com/codenotary/immudb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codenotary/immudb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codenotary/immudb.svg) - immudb is a lightweight, high-speed immutable database for systems and applications written in Go.

It supports fully serializable transactions and many data structures such as  list, set, sorted set.
* [piladb](https://github.com/fern4lvarez/piladb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fern4lvarez/piladb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fern4lvarez/piladb.svg) - Lightweight RESTful database engine based on stack data structures.

On Disk. Eventual consistent. HA. Able to grow or shrink without service interruption.

May be used as long-term remote storage for Prometheus. Supports PromQL.

*Database schema migration.*

* [avro](https://github.com/khezen/avro) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/khezen/avro.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/khezen/avro.svg) - Discover SQL schemas and convert them to AVRO schemas. Query SQL records into AVRO bytes.
* [darwin](https://github.com/GuiaBolso/darwin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/GuiaBolso/darwin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/GuiaBolso/darwin.svg) - Database schema evolution library for Go.
* [go-fixtures](https://github.com/RichardKnop/go-fixtures) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RichardKnop/go-fixtures.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RichardKnop/go-fixtures.svg) - Django style fixtures for Golang's excellent built-in database/sql library.
* [go-pg-migrate](https://github.com/lawzava/go-pg-migrate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lawzava/go-pg-migrate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lawzava/go-pg-migrate.svg) - CLI-friendly package for go-pg migrations management.
* [go-pg-migrations](https://github.com/robinjoseph08/go-pg-migrations) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robinjoseph08/go-pg-migrations.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robinjoseph08/go-pg-migrations.svg) - A Go package to help write migrations with go-pg/pg.
* [goose](https://github.com/pressly/goose) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pressly/goose.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pressly/goose.svg) - Database migration tool. You can manage your database's evolution by creating incremental SQL or Go scripts.
* [gormigrate](https://github.com/go-gormigrate/gormigrate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gormigrate/gormigrate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gormigrate/gormigrate.svg) - Database schema migration helper for Gorm ORM.
* [migrate](https://github.com/golang-migrate/migrate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang-migrate/migrate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang-migrate/migrate.svg) - Database migrations. CLI and Golang library.
* [migrator](https://github.com/lopezator/migrator) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lopezator/migrator.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lopezator/migrator.svg) - Dead simple Go database migration library.
* [migrator](https://github.com/larapulse/migrator) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/larapulse/migrator.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/larapulse/migrator.svg) - MySQL database migrator designed to run migrations to your features and manage database schema update with intuitive go code.
* [pravasan](https://github.com/pravasan/pravasan) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pravasan/pravasan.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pravasan/pravasan.svg) - Simple Migration tool - currently for MySQL but planning to soon support Postgres, SQLite, MongoDB, etc.
* [schema](https://github.com/adlio/schema) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adlio/schema.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adlio/schema.svg) - Library to embed schema migrations for database/sql-compatible databases inside your Go binaries.
* [skeema](https://github.com/skeema/skeema) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skeema/skeema.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skeema/skeema.svg) - Pure-SQL schema management system for MySQL, with support for sharding and external online schema change tools.
* [soda](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop/tree/master/soda) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gobuffalo/pop.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gobuffalo/pop.svg) - Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite.
* [sql-migrate](https://github.com/rubenv/sql-migrate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rubenv/sql-migrate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rubenv/sql-migrate.svg) - Database migration tool. Allows embedding migrations into the application using go-bindata.
* [sqlize](https://github.com/sunary/sqlize) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sunary/sqlize.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sunary/sqlize.svg) - Database migration generator. Allows generate sql migration from model and existing sql by differ them.

*Database tools.*

* [chproxy](https://github.com/Vertamedia/chproxy) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Vertamedia/chproxy.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Vertamedia/chproxy.svg) - HTTP proxy for ClickHouse database.

* [datagen](https://github.com/codingconcepts/datagen) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codingconcepts/datagen.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codingconcepts/datagen.svg) - A fast data generator that's multi-table aware and supports multi-row DML.
* [dbbench](https://github.com/sj14/dbbench) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sj14/dbbench.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sj14/dbbench.svg) - Database benchmarking tool with support for several databases and scripts.

* [kingshard](https://github.com/flike/kingshard) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flike/kingshard.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flike/kingshard.svg) - kingshard is a high performance proxy for MySQL powered by Golang.
* [myreplication](https://github.com/2tvenom/myreplication) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/2tvenom/myreplication.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/2tvenom/myreplication.svg) - MySql binary log replication listener. Supports statement and row based replication.
* [octillery](https://github.com/knocknote/octillery) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knocknote/octillery.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knocknote/octillery.svg) - Go package for sharding databases ( Supports every ORM or raw SQL ).
* [orchestrator](https://github.com/github/orchestrator) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/github/orchestrator.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/github/orchestrator.svg) - MySQL replication topology manager & visualizer.

* [pgweb](https://github.com/sosedoff/pgweb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sosedoff/pgweb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sosedoff/pgweb.svg) - Web-based PostgreSQL database browser.
* [prep](https://github.com/hexdigest/prep) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hexdigest/prep.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hexdigest/prep.svg) - Use prepared SQL statements without changing your code.
* [pREST](https://github.com/prest/prest) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/prest/prest.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/prest/prest.svg) - Simplify and accelerate development, ⚡ instant, realtime, high-performance on any Postgres application, existing or new.
* [rwdb](https://github.com/andizzle/rwdb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andizzle/rwdb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andizzle/rwdb.svg) - rwdb provides read replica capability for multiple database servers setup.
* [vitess](https://github.com/youtube/vitess) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/youtube/vitess.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/youtube/vitess.svg) - vitess provides servers and tools which facilitate scaling of MySQL databases for large scale web services.

*SQL query builder, libraries for building and using SQL.*

* [hasql](https://golang.yandex/hasql) - Library for accessing multi-host SQL database installations.
* [igor](https://github.com/galeone/igor) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/galeone/igor.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/galeone/igor.svg) - Abstraction layer for PostgreSQL that supports advanced functionality and uses gorm-like syntax.
* [jet](https://github.com/go-jet/jet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-jet/jet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-jet/jet.svg) - Framework for writing type-safe SQL queries in Go, with ability to easily convert database query result into desired arbitrary object structure.
* [mpath](https://github.com/spacetab-io/mpath-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spacetab-io/mpath-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spacetab-io/mpath-go.svg) - MPTT (Modified Preorder Tree Traversal) package for SQL records - materialized path realisation.
* [ormlite](https://github.com/pupizoid/ormlite) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pupizoid/ormlite.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pupizoid/ormlite.svg) - Lightweight package containing some ORM-like features and helpers for sqlite databases.
* [ozzo-dbx](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-dbx) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-ozzo/ozzo-dbx.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-ozzo/ozzo-dbx.svg) - Powerful data retrieval methods as well as DB-agnostic query building capabilities.
* [qry](https://github.com/HnH/qry) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HnH/qry.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HnH/qry.svg) - Tool that generates constants from files with raw SQL queries.
* [sq](https://github.com/bokwoon95/go-structured-query) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bokwoon95/go-structured-query.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bokwoon95/go-structured-query.svg) - Type-safe SQL builder and struct mapper for Go.
* [sqlf](https://github.com/leporo/sqlf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/leporo/sqlf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/leporo/sqlf.svg) - Fast SQL query builder.
* [sqlingo](https://github.com/lqs/sqlingo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lqs/sqlingo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lqs/sqlingo.svg) - A lightweight DSL to build SQL in Go.
* [sqrl](https://github.com/elgris/sqrl) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elgris/sqrl.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elgris/sqrl.svg) - SQL query builder, fork of Squirrel with improved performance.
* [Squalus](https://gitlab.com/qosenergy/squalus) - Thin layer over the Go SQL package that makes it easier to perform queries.
* [Squirrel](https://github.com/Masterminds/squirrel) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Masterminds/squirrel.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Masterminds/squirrel.svg) - Go library that helps you build SQL queries.
* [xo](https://github.com/knq/xo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knq/xo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knq/xo.svg) - Generate idiomatic Go code for databases based on existing schema definitions or custom queries supporting PostgreSQL, MySQL, SQLite, Oracle, and Microsoft SQL Server.

## Database Drivers

*Libraries for connecting and operating databases.*

* Relational Databases
    * [avatica](https://github.com/apache/calcite-avatica-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apache/calcite-avatica-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apache/calcite-avatica-go.svg) - Apache Avatica/Phoenix SQL driver for database/sql.
    * [bgc](https://github.com/viant/bgc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/viant/bgc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/viant/bgc.svg) - Datastore Connectivity for BigQuery for go.
    * [firebirdsql](https://github.com/nakagami/firebirdsql) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nakagami/firebirdsql.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nakagami/firebirdsql.svg) - Firebird RDBMS SQL driver for Go.
    * [go-adodb](https://github.com/mattn/go-adodb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/go-adodb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/go-adodb.svg) - Microsoft ActiveX Object DataBase driver for go that uses database/sql.
    * [go-mssqldb](https://github.com/denisenkom/go-mssqldb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/denisenkom/go-mssqldb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/denisenkom/go-mssqldb.svg) - Microsoft MSSQL driver for Go.
    * [go-oci8](https://github.com/mattn/go-oci8) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/go-oci8.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/go-oci8.svg) - Oracle driver for go that uses database/sql.
    * [go-sql-driver/mysql](https://github.com/go-sql-driver/mysql) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-sql-driver/mysql.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-sql-driver/mysql.svg) - MySQL driver for Go.
    * [go-sqlite3](https://github.com/mattn/go-sqlite3) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/go-sqlite3.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/go-sqlite3.svg) - SQLite3 driver for go that uses database/sql.
    * [godror](https://github.com/godror/godror) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/godror/godror.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/godror/godror.svg) - Oracle driver for Go, using the ODPI-C driver.
    * [gofreetds](https://github.com/minus5/gofreetds) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/minus5/gofreetds.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/minus5/gofreetds.svg) - Microsoft MSSQL driver. Go wrapper over [FreeTDS](https://www.freetds.org).
    * [pgx](https://github.com/jackc/pgx) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jackc/pgx.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jackc/pgx.svg) - PostgreSQL driver supporting features beyond those exposed by database/sql.
    * [pig](https://github.com/alexeyco/pig) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexeyco/pig.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexeyco/pig.svg) - Simple [pgx](https://github.com/jackc/pgx) wrapper to execute and [scan](https://github.com/georgysavva/scany) query results easily.
    * [pq](https://github.com/lib/pq) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lib/pq.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lib/pq.svg) - Pure Go Postgres driver for database/sql.
    * [Sqinn-Go](https://github.com/cvilsmeier/sqinn-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cvilsmeier/sqinn-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cvilsmeier/sqinn-go.svg) - SQLite with pure Go.

* Search and Analytic Databases.

## Date and Time

*Libraries for working with dates and times.*

* [carbon](https://github.com/golang-module/carbon) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang-module/carbon.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang-module/carbon.svg) - A simple, semantic and developer-friendly golang package for datetime.
* [carbon](https://github.com/uniplaces/carbon) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uniplaces/carbon.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uniplaces/carbon.svg) - Simple Time extension with a lot of util methods, ported from PHP Carbon library.
* [cronrange](https://github.com/1set/cronrange) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/1set/cronrange.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/1set/cronrange.svg) - Parses Cron-style time range expressions, checks if the given time is within any ranges.
* [date](https://github.com/rickb777/date) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rickb777/date.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rickb777/date.svg) - Augments Time for working with dates, date ranges, time spans, periods, and time-of-day.

Things like Easter, Pentecost, Thanksgiving...

* [go-sunrise](https://github.com/nathan-osman/go-sunrise) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nathan-osman/go-sunrise.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nathan-osman/go-sunrise.svg) - Calculate the sunrise and sunset times for a given location.

## Dynamic DNS

*Tools for updating dynamic DNS records.*

* [DDNS](https://github.com/skibish/ddns) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skibish/ddns.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skibish/ddns.svg) - Personal DDNS client with Digital Ocean Networking DNS as backend.
* [dyndns](https://gitlab.com/alcastle/dyndns) - Background Go process to regularly and automatically check your IP Address and make updates to (one or many) Dynamic DNS records for Google domains whenever your address changes.

## Embeddable Scripting Languages

* [anko](https://github.com/mattn/anko) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/anko.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/anko.svg) - Scriptable interpreter written in Go.

## Error Handling

*Libraries for handling errors.*

* [emperror](https://github.com/emperror/emperror) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emperror/emperror.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emperror/emperror.svg) - Error handling tools and best practices for Go libraries and applications.
* [eris](https://github.com/rotisserie/eris) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rotisserie/eris.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rotisserie/eris.svg) - A better way to handle, trace, and log errors in Go. Compatible with the standard error library and github.com/pkg/errors.
* [errlog](https://github.com/snwfdhmp/errlog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/snwfdhmp/errlog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/snwfdhmp/errlog.svg) - Hackable package that determines responsible source code for an error (and some other fast-debugging features). Pluggable to any logger in-place.
* [errors](https://github.com/emperror/errors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emperror/errors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emperror/errors.svg) - Drop-in replacement for the standard library errors package and github.com/pkg/errors. Provides various error handling primitives.
* [errors](https://github.com/pkg/errors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkg/errors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkg/errors.svg) - Package that provides simple error handling primitives.
* [errors](https://github.com/neuronlabs/errors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neuronlabs/errors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neuronlabs/errors.svg) - Simple golang error handling with classification primitives.
* [errors](https://github.com/PumpkinSeed/errors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PumpkinSeed/errors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PumpkinSeed/errors.svg) - The most simple error wrapper with awesome performance and minimal memory overhead.
* [errors](https://github.com/bnkamalesh/errors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bnkamalesh/errors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bnkamalesh/errors.svg) - Drop-in replacement for builting Go errors. This is a minimal error handling package with custom error types, user friendly messages, Unwrap & Is. With very easy to use and straightforward helper functions.
* [errorx](https://github.com/joomcode/errorx) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joomcode/errorx.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joomcode/errorx.svg) - A feature rich error package with stack traces, composition of errors and more.
* [Falcon](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/falcon) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SonicRoshan/falcon.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SonicRoshan/falcon.svg) - A Simple Yet Highly Powerful Package For Error Handling.
* [go-multierror](https://github.com/hashicorp/go-multierror) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashicorp/go-multierror.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashicorp/go-multierror.svg) - Go (golang) package for representing a list of errors as a single error.

## Forms

* [bind](https://github.com/robfig/bind) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robfig/bind.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/robfig/bind.svg) - Bind form data to any Go values.

## Goroutines

* [ants](https://github.com/panjf2000/ants) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/panjf2000/ants.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/panjf2000/ants.svg) - A high-performance and low-cost goroutine pool in Go.

* [async](https://github.com/reugn/async) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reugn/async.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reugn/async.svg) - An alternative sync library for Go (Future, Promise, Locks).
* [async](https://github.com/studiosol/async) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/studiosol/async.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/studiosol/async.svg) - A safe way to execute functions asynchronously, recovering them in case of panic.
* [breaker](https://github.com/kamilsk/breaker) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamilsk/breaker.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamilsk/breaker.svg) - Flexible mechanism to make execution flow interruptible.
* [channelify](https://github.com/ddelizia/channelify) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ddelizia/channelify.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ddelizia/channelify.svg) - Transform your function to return channels for easy and powerful parallel processing.
* [concurrency-limiter](https://github.com/vivek-ng/concurrency-limiter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vivek-ng/concurrency-limiter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vivek-ng/concurrency-limiter.svg) - Concurrency limiter with support for timeouts , dynamic priority and context cancellation of goroutines.
* [conexec](https://github.com/ITcathyh/conexec) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ITcathyh/conexec.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ITcathyh/conexec.svg) - A concurrent toolkit to help execute funcs concurrently in an efficient and safe way. It supports specifying the overall timeout to avoid blocking and uses goroutine pool to improve efficiency.
* [cyclicbarrier](https://github.com/marusama/cyclicbarrier) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marusama/cyclicbarrier.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marusama/cyclicbarrier.svg) - CyclicBarrier for golang.
* [execpool](https://github.com/hexdigest/execpool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hexdigest/execpool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hexdigest/execpool.svg) - A pool built around exec.Cmd that spins up a given number of processes in advance and attaches stdin and stdout to them when needed. Very similar to FastCGI or Apache Prefork MPM but works for any command.
* [go-floc](https://github.com/workanator/go-floc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/workanator/go-floc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/workanator/go-floc.svg) - Orchestrate goroutines with ease.
* [go-flow](https://github.com/kamildrazkiewicz/go-flow) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamildrazkiewicz/go-flow.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamildrazkiewicz/go-flow.svg) - Control goroutines execution order.
* [go-tools/multithreading](https://github.com/nikhilsaraf/go-tools) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikhilsaraf/go-tools.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikhilsaraf/go-tools.svg) - Manage a pool of goroutines using this lightweight library with a simple API.
* [go-trylock](https://github.com/subchen/go-trylock) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subchen/go-trylock.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subchen/go-trylock.svg) - TryLock support on read-write lock for Golang.

* [go-workers](https://github.com/catmullet/go-workers) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/catmullet/go-workers.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/catmullet/go-workers.svg) - Easily and safely run workers for large data processing pipelines.
* [goccm](https://github.com/zenthangplus/goccm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zenthangplus/goccm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zenthangplus/goccm.svg) - Go Concurrency Manager package limits the number of goroutines that allowed to run concurrently.
* [gohive](https://github.com/loveleshsharma/gohive) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/loveleshsharma/gohive.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/loveleshsharma/gohive.svg) - A highly performant and easy to use Goroutine pool for Go.
* [gollback](https://github.com/vardius/gollback) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vardius/gollback.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vardius/gollback.svg) - asynchronous simple function utilities, for managing execution of closures and callbacks.
* [gowl](https://github.com/hamed-yousefi/gowl) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hamed-yousefi/gowl.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hamed-yousefi/gowl.svg) - Gowl is a process management and process monitoring tool at once. An infinite worker pool gives you the ability to control the pool and processes and monitor their status.
* [goworker](https://github.com/benmanns/goworker) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benmanns/goworker.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benmanns/goworker.svg) - goworker is a Go-based background worker.
* [gowp](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gowp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xxjwxc/gowp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xxjwxc/gowp.svg) - gowp is concurrency limiting goroutine pool.
* [gpool](https://github.com/Sherifabdlnaby/gpool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Sherifabdlnaby/gpool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Sherifabdlnaby/gpool.svg) - manages a resizeable pool of context-aware goroutines to bound concurrency.
* [grpool](https://github.com/ivpusic/grpool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivpusic/grpool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivpusic/grpool.svg) - Lightweight Goroutine pool.
* [hands](https://github.com/duanckham/hands) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/duanckham/hands.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/duanckham/hands.svg) - A process controller used to control the execution and return strategies of multiple goroutines.
* [Hunch](https://github.com/AaronJan/Hunch) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AaronJan/Hunch.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AaronJan/Hunch.svg) - Hunch provides functions like: `All`, `First`, `Retry`, `Waterfall` etc., that makes asynchronous flow control more intuitive.
* [kyoo](https://github.com/dirkaholic/kyoo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dirkaholic/kyoo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dirkaholic/kyoo.svg) - Provides an unlimited job queue and concurrent worker pools.
* [neilotoole/errgroup](https://github.com/neilotoole/errgroup) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neilotoole/errgroup.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neilotoole/errgroup.svg) - Drop-in alternative to `sync/errgroup`, limited to a pool of N worker goroutines.
* [nursery](https://github.com/arunsworld/nursery) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arunsworld/nursery.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arunsworld/nursery.svg) - Structured concurrency in Go.
* [oversight](https://cirello.io/oversight) - Oversight is a complete implementation of the Erlang supervision trees.
* [parallel-fn](https://github.com/rafaeljesus/parallel-fn) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rafaeljesus/parallel-fn.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rafaeljesus/parallel-fn.svg) - Run functions in parallel.
* [pond](https://github.com/alitto/pond) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alitto/pond.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alitto/pond.svg) - Minimalistic and High-performance goroutine worker pool written in Go.
* [pool](https://github.com/go-playground/pool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/pool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/pool.svg) - Limited consumer goroutine or unlimited goroutine pool for easier goroutine handling and cancellation.
* [queue](https://github.com/AnikHasibul/queue) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AnikHasibul/queue.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AnikHasibul/queue.svg) - Gives you a `sync.WaitGroup` like queue group accessibility. Helps you to throttle and limit goroutines, wait for the end of the all goroutines and much more.
* [routine](https://github.com/x-mod/routine) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/x-mod/routine.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/x-mod/routine.svg) - go routine control with context, support: Main, Go, Pool and some useful Executors.
* [semaphore](https://github.com/kamilsk/semaphore) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamilsk/semaphore.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamilsk/semaphore.svg) - Semaphore pattern implementation with timeout of lock/unlock operations based on channel and context.
* [semaphore](https://github.com/marusama/semaphore) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marusama/semaphore.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marusama/semaphore.svg) - Fast resizable semaphore implementation based on CAS (faster than channel-based semaphore implementations).
* [stl](https://github.com/ssgreg/stl) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ssgreg/stl.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ssgreg/stl.svg) - Software transactional locks based on Software Transactional Memory (STM) concurrency control mechanism.
* [threadpool](https://github.com/shettyh/threadpool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shettyh/threadpool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shettyh/threadpool.svg) - Golang threadpool implementation.
* [tunny](https://github.com/Jeffail/tunny) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Jeffail/tunny.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Jeffail/tunny.svg) - Goroutine pool for golang.
* [worker-pool](https://github.com/vardius/worker-pool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vardius/worker-pool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vardius/worker-pool.svg) - goworker is a Go simple async worker pool.
* [workerpool](https://github.com/gammazero/workerpool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gammazero/workerpool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gammazero/workerpool.svg) - Goroutine pool that limits the concurrency of task execution, not the number of tasks queued.

**[⬆ back to top](#contents)**

## Job Scheduler

*Libraries for scheduling jobs.*

* [clockwerk](https://github.com/onatm/clockwerk) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onatm/clockwerk.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/onatm/clockwerk.svg) - Go package to schedule periodic jobs using a simple, fluent syntax.
* [cronticker](https://github.com/krayzpipes/cronticker) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krayzpipes/cronticker.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/krayzpipes/cronticker.svg) - A ticker implementation to support cron schedules.
* [go-cron](https://github.com/rk/go-cron) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rk/go-cron.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rk/go-cron.svg) - Simple Cron library for go that can execute closures or functions at varying intervals, from once a second to once a year on a specific date and time. Primarily for web applications and long running daemons.
* [go-quartz](https://github.com/reugn/go-quartz) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reugn/go-quartz.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reugn/go-quartz.svg) - Simple, zero-dependency scheduling library for Go.
* [gocron](https://github.com/go-co-op/gocron) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-co-op/gocron.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-co-op/gocron.svg) - Easy and fluent Go job scheduling. This is an actively maintained fork of [jasonlvhit/gocron](https://github.com/jasonlvhit/gocron).
* [gron](https://github.com/roylee0704/gron) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roylee0704/gron.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roylee0704/gron.svg) - Define time-based tasks using a simple Go API and Gron’s scheduler will run them accordingly.
* [gronx](https://github.com/adhocore/gronx) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adhocore/gronx.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adhocore/gronx.svg) - Cron expression parser, task runner and daemon consuming crontab like task list.
* [JobRunner](https://github.com/bamzi/jobrunner) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bamzi/jobrunner.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bamzi/jobrunner.svg) - Smart and featureful cron job scheduler with job queuing and live monitoring built in.
* [jobs](https://github.com/albrow/jobs) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/albrow/jobs.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/albrow/jobs.svg) - Persistent and flexible background jobs library.
* [leprechaun](https://github.com/kilgaloon/leprechaun) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kilgaloon/leprechaun.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kilgaloon/leprechaun.svg) - Job scheduler that supports webhooks, crons and classic scheduling.
* [sched](https://github.com/romshark/sched) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romshark/sched.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romshark/sched.svg) - A job scheduler with the ability to fast-forward time.
* [scheduler](https://github.com/carlescere/scheduler) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carlescere/scheduler.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carlescere/scheduler.svg) - Cronjobs scheduling made easy.
* [tasks](https://github.com/madflojo/tasks) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/madflojo/tasks.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/madflojo/tasks.svg) - An easy to use in-process scheduler for recurring tasks in Go.

**[⬆ back to top](#contents)**

## JSON

*Libraries for working with JSON.*

* [ajson](https://github.com/spyzhov/ajson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spyzhov/ajson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spyzhov/ajson.svg) - Abstract JSON for golang with JSONPath support.
* [ask](https://github.com/simonnilsson/ask) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simonnilsson/ask.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/simonnilsson/ask.svg) - Easy access to nested values in maps and slices. Works in combination with encoding/json and other packages that "Unmarshal" arbitrary data into Go data-types.
* [dynjson](https://github.com/cocoonspace/dynjson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cocoonspace/dynjson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cocoonspace/dynjson.svg) - Client-customizable JSON formats for dynamic APIs.
* [ej](https://github.com/lucassscaravelli/ej) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lucassscaravelli/ej.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lucassscaravelli/ej.svg) - Write and read JSON from different sources succinctly.
* [epoch](https://github.com/vtopc/epoch) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vtopc/epoch.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vtopc/epoch.svg) - Contains primitives for marshaling/unmarshaling Unix timestamp/epoch to/from build-in time.Time type in JSON.
* [fastjson](https://github.com/valyala/fastjson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/fastjson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/fastjson.svg) - Fast JSON parser and validator for Go. No custom structs, no code generation, no reflection.
* [gjo](https://github.com/skanehira/gjo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skanehira/gjo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/skanehira/gjo.svg) - Small utility to create JSON objects.
* [GJSON](https://github.com/tidwall/gjson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tidwall/gjson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tidwall/gjson.svg) - Get a JSON value with one line of code.
* [go-jsonerror](https://github.com/ddymko/go-jsonerror) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ddymko/go-jsonerror.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ddymko/go-jsonerror.svg) - Go-JsonError is ment to allow us to easily create json response errors that follow the JsonApi spec.
* [go-respond](https://github.com/nicklaw5/go-respond) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nicklaw5/go-respond.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nicklaw5/go-respond.svg) - Go package for handling common HTTP JSON responses.
* [gojq](https://github.com/elgs/gojq) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elgs/gojq.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elgs/gojq.svg) - JSON query in Golang.
* [gojson](https://github.com/ChimeraCoder/gojson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChimeraCoder/gojson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChimeraCoder/gojson.svg) - Automatically generate Go (golang) struct definitions from example JSON.
* [JayDiff](https://github.com/yazgazan/jaydiff) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yazgazan/jaydiff.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yazgazan/jaydiff.svg) - JSON diff utility written in Go.
* [jettison](https://github.com/wI2L/jettison) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wI2L/jettison.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wI2L/jettison.svg) - Fast and flexible JSON encoder for Go.
* [JSON-to-Go](https://mholt.github.io/json-to-go/) - Convert JSON to Go struct.
* [JSON-to-Proto](https://json-to-proto.github.io/) - Convert JSON to Protobuf online.
* [json2go](https://github.com/m-zajac/json2go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m-zajac/json2go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m-zajac/json2go.svg) - Advanced JSON to Go struct conversion. Provides package that can parse multiple JSON documents and create struct to fit them all.
* [jsonapi-errors](https://github.com/AmuzaTkts/jsonapi-errors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AmuzaTkts/jsonapi-errors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AmuzaTkts/jsonapi-errors.svg) - Go bindings based on the JSON API errors reference.
* [jsoncolor](https://github.com/neilotoole/jsoncolor) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neilotoole/jsoncolor.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neilotoole/jsoncolor.svg) - Drop-in replacement for `encoding/json` that outputs colorized JSON.
* [jsondiff](https://github.com/wI2L/jsondiff) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wI2L/jsondiff.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wI2L/jsondiff.svg) - JSON diff library for Go based on RFC6902 (JSON Patch).
* [jsonf](https://github.com/miolini/jsonf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miolini/jsonf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miolini/jsonf.svg) - Console tool for highlighted formatting and struct query fetching JSON.
* [jsongo](https://github.com/ricardolonga/jsongo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ricardolonga/jsongo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ricardolonga/jsongo.svg) - Fluent API to make it easier to create Json objects.
* [jsonhal](https://github.com/RichardKnop/jsonhal) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RichardKnop/jsonhal.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RichardKnop/jsonhal.svg) - Simple Go package to make custom structs marshal into HAL compatible JSON responses.
* [jsonic](https://github.com/sinhashubham95/jsonic) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sinhashubham95/jsonic.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sinhashubham95/jsonic.svg) - Utilities to handle and query JSON without defining structs in a type safe manner.
* [jzon](https://github.com/zerosnake0/jzon) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zerosnake0/jzon.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zerosnake0/jzon.svg) - JSON library with standard compatible API/behavior.
* [kazaam](https://github.com/Qntfy/kazaam) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Qntfy/kazaam.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Qntfy/kazaam.svg) - API for arbitrary transformation of JSON documents.
* [mapslice-json](https://github.com/mickep76/mapslice-json) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mickep76/mapslice-json.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mickep76/mapslice-json.svg) - Go MapSlice for ordered marshal/ unmarshal of maps in JSON.
* [mp](https://github.com/sanbornm/mp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sanbornm/mp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sanbornm/mp.svg) - Simple cli email parser. It currently takes stdin and outputs JSON.
* [OjG](https://github.com/ohler55/ojg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ohler55/ojg.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ohler55/ojg.svg) - Optimized JSON for Go is a high performance parser with a variety of additional JSON tools including JSONPath.
* [omg.jsonparser](https://github.com/dedalqq/omg.jsonparser) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dedalqq/omg.jsonparser.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dedalqq/omg.jsonparser.svg) - Simple JSON parser with validation by condition via golang struct fields tags.
* [ujson](https://github.com/olvrng/ujson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olvrng/ujson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/olvrng/ujson.svg) - Fast and minimal JSON parser and transformer that works on unstructured JSON.
* [vjson](https://github.com/miladibra10/vjson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miladibra10/vjson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miladibra10/vjson.svg) - Go package for validating JSON objects with declaring a JSON schema with fluent API.
