## Logging

*Libraries for generating and working with log files.*

* [distillog](https://github.com/amoghe/distillog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/amoghe/distillog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/amoghe/distillog.svg) - distilled levelled logging (think of it as stdlib + log levels).
* [glg](https://github.com/kpango/glg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kpango/glg.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kpango/glg.svg) - glg is simple and fast leveled logging library for Go.
* [glo](https://github.com/lajosbencz/glo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lajosbencz/glo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lajosbencz/glo.svg) - PHP Monolog inspired logging facility with identical severity levels.
* [glog](https://github.com/golang/glog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/glog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/glog.svg) - Leveled execution logs for Go.
* [go-cronowriter](https://github.com/utahta/go-cronowriter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/utahta/go-cronowriter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/utahta/go-cronowriter.svg) - Simple writer that rotate log files automatically based on current date and time, like cronolog.
* [go-log](https://github.com/pieterclaerhout/go-log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pieterclaerhout/go-log.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pieterclaerhout/go-log.svg) - A logging library with strack traces, object dumping and optional timestamps.
* [go-log](https://github.com/subchen/go-log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subchen/go-log.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/subchen/go-log.svg) - Simple and configurable Logging in Go, with level, formatters and writers.
* [go-log](https://github.com/siddontang/go-log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/siddontang/go-log.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/siddontang/go-log.svg) - Log lib supports level and multi handlers.
* [go-log](https://github.com/ian-kent/go-log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ian-kent/go-log.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ian-kent/go-log.svg) - Log4j implementation in Go.
* [go-logger](https://github.com/apsdehal/go-logger) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apsdehal/go-logger.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/apsdehal/go-logger.svg) - Simple logger of Go Programs, with level handlers.
* [gologger](https://github.com/sadlil/gologger) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sadlil/gologger.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sadlil/gologger.svg) - Simple easy to use log lib for go, logs in Colored Console, Simple Console, File or Elasticsearch.
* [gomol](https://github.com/aphistic/gomol) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aphistic/gomol.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aphistic/gomol.svg) - Multiple-output, structured logging for Go with extensible logging outputs.
* [gone/log](https://github.com/One-com/gone/tree/master/log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/One-com/gone.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/One-com/gone.svg) - Fast, extendable, full-featured, std-lib source compatible log library.
* [httpretty](https://github.com/henvic/httpretty) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/henvic/httpretty.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/henvic/httpretty.svg) - Pretty-prints your regular HTTP requests on your terminal for debugging (similar to http.DumpRequest).
* [journald](https://github.com/ssgreg/journald) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ssgreg/journald.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ssgreg/journald.svg) - Go implementation of systemd Journal's native API for logging.

* [noodlog](https://github.com/gyozatech/noodlog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gyozatech/noodlog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gyozatech/noodlog.svg) - Parametrized JSON logging library which lets you obfuscate sensitive data and marshal any kind of content. No more printed pointers instead of values, nor escape chars for the JSON strings.
* [onelog](https://github.com/francoispqt/onelog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/francoispqt/onelog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/francoispqt/onelog.svg) - Onelog is a dead simple but very efficient JSON logger. It is the fastest JSON logger out there in all scenarios. Also, it is one of the logger with the lowest allocation.
* [ozzo-log](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-ozzo/ozzo-log.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-ozzo/ozzo-log.svg) - High performance logging supporting log severity, categorization, and filtering. * [stdlog](https://github.com/alexcesaro/log) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexcesaro/log.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexcesaro/log.svg) - Stdlog is an object-oriented library providing leveled logging. It is very useful for cron jobs.
* [tail](https://github.com/hpcloud/tail) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hpcloud/tail.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hpcloud/tail.svg) - Go package striving to emulate the features of the BSD tail program.
* [xlog](https://github.com/xfxdev/xlog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xfxdev/xlog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xfxdev/xlog.svg) - Plugin architecture and flexible log system for Go, with level ctrl, multiple log target and custom log format.

* [rmqconn](https://github.com/sbabiv/rmqconn) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sbabiv/rmqconn.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sbabiv/rmqconn.svg) - RabbitMQ Reconnection. Wrapper over amqp.Connection and amqp.Dial. Allowing to do a reconnection when the connection is broken before forcing the call to the Close () method to be closed.
* [sarama](https://github.com/Shopify/sarama) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Shopify/sarama.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Shopify/sarama.svg) - Go library for Apache Kafka.
* [Uniqush-Push](https://github.com/uniqush/uniqush-push) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uniqush/uniqush-push.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uniqush/uniqush-push.svg) - Redis backed unified push service for server-side notifications to mobile devices.
* [zmq4](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq4) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pebbe/zmq4.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pebbe/zmq4.svg) - Go interface to ZeroMQ version 4. Also available for [version 3](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq3) and [version 2](https://github.com/pebbe/zmq2).

* [xkg](https://github.com/go-xkg/xkg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-xkg/xkg.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-xkg/xkg.svg) - X Keyboard Grabber.

## Natural Language Processing

Supports batch requests, short phrase or single word language detection.
* [getlang](https://github.com/rylans/getlang) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rylans/getlang.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rylans/getlang.svg) - Fast natural language detection package.

* [go-mystem](https://github.com/dveselov/mystem) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dveselov/mystem.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dveselov/mystem.svg) - CGo bindings to Yandex.Mystem - russian morphology analyzer.

(Now only support chinese segmentation)

## Networking

*Libraries for working with various layers of the network.*

* [arp](https://github.com/mdlayher/arp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/arp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/arp.svg) - Package arp implements the ARP protocol, as described in RFC 826.
* [buffstreams](https://github.com/stabbycutyou/buffstreams) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stabbycutyou/buffstreams.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stabbycutyou/buffstreams.svg) - Streaming protocolbuffer data over TCP made easy.
* [canopus](https://github.com/zubairhamed/canopus) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zubairhamed/canopus.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zubairhamed/canopus.svg) - CoAP Client/Server implementation (RFC 7252).
* [cidranger](https://github.com/yl2chen/cidranger) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yl2chen/cidranger.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yl2chen/cidranger.svg) - Fast IP to CIDR lookup for Go.
* [dhcp6](https://github.com/mdlayher/dhcp6) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/dhcp6.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/dhcp6.svg) - Package dhcp6 implements a DHCPv6 server, as described in RFC 3315.
* [dns](https://github.com/miekg/dns) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miekg/dns.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miekg/dns.svg) - Go library for working with DNS.
* [easytcp](https://github.com/DarthPestilane/easytcp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DarthPestilane/easytcp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DarthPestilane/easytcp.svg) - A light-weight TCP framework written in Go (Golang), built with message router. EasyTCP helps you build a TCP server easily fast and less painful.
* [ether](https://github.com/songgao/ether) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/songgao/ether.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/songgao/ether.svg) - Cross-platform Go package for sending and receiving ethernet frames.
* [ethernet](https://github.com/mdlayher/ethernet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/ethernet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/ethernet.svg) - Package ethernet implements marshaling and unmarshaling of IEEE 802.3 Ethernet II frames and IEEE 802.1Q VLAN tags.
* [fasthttp](https://github.com/valyala/fasthttp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/fasthttp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/fasthttp.svg) - Package fasthttp is a fast HTTP implementation for Go, up to 10 times faster than net/http.
* [fortio](https://github.com/fortio/fortio) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fortio/fortio.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fortio/fortio.svg) - Load testing library and command line tool, advanced echo server and web UI. Allows to specify a set query-per-second load and record latency histograms and other useful stats and graph them. Tcp, Http, gRPC.
* [ftp](https://github.com/jlaffaye/ftp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jlaffaye/ftp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jlaffaye/ftp.svg) - Package ftp implements a FTP client as described in [RFC 959](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc959).
* [ftpserverlib](https://github.com/fclairamb/ftpserverlib) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fclairamb/ftpserverlib.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fclairamb/ftpserverlib.svg) - Fully featured FTP server library.
* [gaio](https://github.com/xtaci/gaio) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xtaci/gaio.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xtaci/gaio.svg) - High performance async-io networking for Golang in proactor mode.
* [gev](https://github.com/Allenxuxu/gev) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Allenxuxu/gev.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Allenxuxu/gev.svg) - gev is a lightweight, fast non-blocking TCP network library based on Reactor mode.
* [gmqtt](https://github.com/DrmagicE/gmqtt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DrmagicE/gmqtt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DrmagicE/gmqtt.svg) - Gmqtt is a flexible, high-performance MQTT broker library that fully implements the MQTT protocol V3.1.1.
* [gnet](https://github.com/panjf2000/gnet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/panjf2000/gnet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/panjf2000/gnet.svg) - `gnet` is a high-performance, lightweight, non-blocking, event-driven networking framework written in pure Go.
* [gNxI](https://github.com/google/gnxi) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/gnxi.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/gnxi.svg) - A collection of tools for Network Management that use the gNMI and gNOI protocols.

* [mdns](https://github.com/hashicorp/mdns) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashicorp/mdns.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashicorp/mdns.svg) - Simple mDNS (Multicast DNS) client/server library in Golang.
* [mqttPaho](https://eclipse.org/paho/clients/golang/) - The Paho Go Client provides an MQTT client library for connection to MQTT brokers via TCP, TLS or WebSockets.
* [nbio](https://github.com/lesismal/nbio) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lesismal/nbio.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lesismal/nbio.svg) - High-performance, non-blocking, event-driven, easy-to-use, least-dependency networking framework written in Go.
* [NFF-Go](https://github.com/intel-go/nff-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/intel-go/nff-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/intel-go/nff-go.svg) - Framework for rapid development of performant network functions for cloud and bare-metal (former YANFF).
* [packet](https://github.com/aerogo/packet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aerogo/packet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aerogo/packet.svg) - Send packets over TCP and UDP. It can buffer messages and hot-swap connections if needed.
* [panoptes-stream](https://github.com/yahoo/panoptes-stream) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoo/panoptes-stream.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoo/panoptes-stream.svg) - A cloud native distributed streaming network telemetry (gNMI, Juniper JTI and Cisco MDT).
* [peerdiscovery](https://github.com/schollz/peerdiscovery) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/schollz/peerdiscovery.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/schollz/peerdiscovery.svg) - Pure Go library for cross-platform local peer discovery using UDP multicast.
* [portproxy](https://github.com/aybabtme/portproxy) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aybabtme/portproxy.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aybabtme/portproxy.svg) - Simple TCP proxy which adds CORS support to API's which don't support it.
* [publicip](https://github.com/polera/publicip) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/polera/publicip.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/polera/publicip.svg) - Package publicip returns your public facing IPv4 address (internet egress).
* [quic-go](https://github.com/lucas-clemente/quic-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lucas-clemente/quic-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lucas-clemente/quic-go.svg) - An implementation of the QUIC protocol in pure Go.
* [raw](https://github.com/mdlayher/raw) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/raw.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdlayher/raw.svg) - Package raw enables reading and writing data at the device driver level for a network interface.
* [sftp](https://github.com/pkg/sftp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkg/sftp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkg/sftp.svg) - Package sftp implements the SSH File Transfer Protocol as described in https://filezilla-project.org/specs/draft-ietf-secsh-filexfer-02.txt.
* [ssh](https://github.com/gliderlabs/ssh) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gliderlabs/ssh.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gliderlabs/ssh.svg) - Higher-level API for building SSH servers (wraps crypto/ssh).
* [sslb](https://github.com/eduardonunesp/sslb) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eduardonunesp/sslb.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eduardonunesp/sslb.svg) - It's a Super Simples Load Balancer, just a little project to achieve some kind of performance.
* [stun](https://github.com/go-rtc/stun) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-rtc/stun.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-rtc/stun.svg) - Go implementation of RFC 5389 STUN protocol.
* [tcp_server](https://github.com/firstrow/tcp_server) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/firstrow/tcp_server.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/firstrow/tcp_server.svg) - Go library for building tcp servers faster.
* [tspool](https://github.com/two/tspool) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/two/tspool.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/two/tspool.svg) - A TCP Library use worker pool to improve performance and protect your server.
* [utp](https://github.com/anacrolix/utp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/anacrolix/utp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/anacrolix/utp.svg) - Go uTP micro transport protocol implementation.
* [vssh](https://github.com/yahoo/vssh) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoo/vssh.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yahoo/vssh.svg) - Go library for building network and server automation over SSH protocol.
* [water](https://github.com/songgao/water) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/songgao/water.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/songgao/water.svg) - Simple TUN/TAP library.
* [webrtc](https://github.com/pions/webrtc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pions/webrtc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pions/webrtc.svg) - A pure Go implementation of the WebRTC API.
* [winrm](https://github.com/masterzen/winrm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/masterzen/winrm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/masterzen/winrm.svg) - Go WinRM client to remotely execute commands on Windows machines.
* [xtcp](https://github.com/xfxdev/xtcp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xfxdev/xtcp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xfxdev/xtcp.svg) - TCP Server Framework with simultaneous full duplex communication, graceful shutdown, and custom protocol.

### HTTP Clients

* [httpc](https://github.com/valord577/httpc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valord577/httpc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valord577/httpc.svg) - A customizable and simple HTTP client library. Only depend on the stdlib HTTP client.
* [httpretry](https://github.com/ybbus/httpretry) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ybbus/httpretry.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ybbus/httpretry.svg) - Enriches the default go HTTP client with retry functionality.
* [pester](https://github.com/sethgrid/pester) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sethgrid/pester.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sethgrid/pester.svg) - Go HTTP client calls with retries, backoff, and concurrency.
* [request](https://github.com/monaco-io/request) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/monaco-io/request.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/monaco-io/request.svg) - HTTP client for golang. If you have experience about axios or requests, you will love it. No 3rd dependency.
* [requests](https://github.com/carlmjohnson/requests) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carlmjohnson/requests.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carlmjohnson/requests.svg) - HTTP requests for Gophers. Uses context.Context and doesn't hide the underlying net/http.Client, making it compatible with standard Go APIs. Also includes testing tools.
* [resty](https://github.com/go-resty/resty) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-resty/resty.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-resty/resty.svg) - Simple HTTP and REST client for Go inspired by Ruby rest-client.
* [rq](https://github.com/ddo/rq) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ddo/rq.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ddo/rq.svg) - A nicer interface for golang stdlib HTTP client.

## ORM

* [beego orm](https://github.com/beego/beego) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/beego/beego.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/beego/beego.svg) - Powerful orm framework for go. Support: pq/mysql/sqlite3.

* [go-sql](https://github.com/rushteam/gosql) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rushteam/gosql.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rushteam/gosql.svg) - A easy ORM for mysql.

* [go-store](https://github.com/gosuri/go-store) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gosuri/go-store.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gosuri/go-store.svg) - Simple and fast Redis backed key-value store library for Go.
* [GORM](https://github.com/go-gorm/gorm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gorm/gorm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gorm/gorm.svg) - The fantastic ORM library for Golang, aims to be developer friendly.
* [gormt](https://github.com/xxjwxc/gormt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xxjwxc/gormt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xxjwxc/gormt.svg) - Mysql database to golang gorm struct.
* [gorp](https://github.com/go-gorp/gorp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gorp/gorp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-gorp/gorp.svg) - Go Relational Persistence, ORM-ish library for Go.
* [grimoire](https://github.com/Fs02/grimoire) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Fs02/grimoire.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Fs02/grimoire.svg) - Grimoire is a database access layer and validation for golang. (Support: MySQL, PostgreSQL and SQLite3).
* [lore](https://github.com/abrahambotros/lore) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abrahambotros/lore.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/abrahambotros/lore.svg) - Simple and lightweight pseudo-ORM/pseudo-struct-mapping environment for Go.
* [marlow](https://github.com/marlow/marlow) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marlow/marlow.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/marlow/marlow.svg) - Generated ORM from project structs for compile time safety assurances.
* [pop/soda](https://github.com/gobuffalo/pop) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gobuffalo/pop.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gobuffalo/pop.svg) - Database migration, creation, ORM, etc... for MySQL, PostgreSQL, and SQLite.
* [reform](https://github.com/go-reform/reform) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-reform/reform.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-reform/reform.svg) - Better ORM for Go, based on non-empty interfaces and code generation.
* [rel](https://github.com/go-rel/rel) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-rel/rel.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-rel/rel.svg) - Modern Database Access Layer for Golang - Testable, Extendable and Crafted Into a Clean and Elegant API.

## Package Management

*Official tooling for dependency and package management*

* [go modules](https://golang.org/cmd/go/#hdr-Modules__module_versions__and_more) - Modules are the unit of source code interchange and versioning. The go command has direct support for working with modules, including recording and resolving dependencies on other modules.

*Official experimental tooling for package management*

* [dep](https://github.com/golang/dep) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/dep.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/dep.svg) - Go dependency tool.
* [vgo](https://go.googlesource.com/vgo/) - Versioned Go.

*Unofficial libraries for package and dependency management.*

* [glide](https://github.com/Masterminds/glide) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Masterminds/glide.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Masterminds/glide.svg) - Manage your golang vendor and vendored packages with ease. Inspired by tools like Maven, Bundler, and Pip.
* [godep](https://github.com/tools/godep) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tools/godep.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tools/godep.svg) - dependency tool for go, godep helps build packages reproducibly by fixing their dependencies.
* [gom](https://github.com/mattn/gom) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/gom.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mattn/gom.svg) - Go Manager - bundle for go.
* [goop](https://github.com/nitrous-io/goop) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nitrous-io/goop.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nitrous-io/goop.svg) - Simple dependency manager for Go (golang), inspired by Bundler.
* [gop](https://github.com/lunny/gop) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lunny/gop.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lunny/gop.svg) - Build and manage your Go applications out of GOPATH.
* [gopm](https://github.com/gpmgo/gopm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gpmgo/gopm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gpmgo/gopm.svg) - Go Package Manager.
* [govendor](https://github.com/kardianos/govendor) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kardianos/govendor.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kardianos/govendor.svg) - Go Package Manager. Go vendor tool that works with the standard vendor file.
* [gpm](https://github.com/pote/gpm) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pote/gpm.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pote/gpm.svg) - Barebones dependency manager for Go.
* [johnny-deps](https://github.com/VividCortex/johnny-deps) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VividCortex/johnny-deps.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VividCortex/johnny-deps.svg) - Minimal dependency version using Git.
* [modgv](https://github.com/lucasepe/modgv) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lucasepe/modgv.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lucasepe/modgv.svg) - Converts 'go mod graph' output into Graphviz's DOT language.
* [mvn-golang](https://github.com/raydac/mvn-golang) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/raydac/mvn-golang.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/raydac/mvn-golang.svg) - plugin that provides way for auto-loading of Golang SDK, dependency management and start build environment in Maven project infrastructure.
* [nut](https://github.com/jingweno/nut) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jingweno/nut.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jingweno/nut.svg) - Vendor Go dependencies.
* [VenGO](https://github.com/DamnWidget/VenGO) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DamnWidget/VenGO.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DamnWidget/VenGO.svg) - create and manage exportable isolated go virtual environments.

## Query Language

* [api-fu](https://github.com/ccbrown/api-fu) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ccbrown/api-fu.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ccbrown/api-fu.svg) - Comprehensive GraphQL implementation.
* [dasel](https://github.com/tomwright/dasel) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomwright/dasel.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tomwright/dasel.svg) - Query and update data structures using selectors from the command line. Comparable to jq/yq but supports JSON, YAML, TOML and XML with zero runtime dependencies.
* [gojsonq](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/gojsonq) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thedevsaddam/gojsonq.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thedevsaddam/gojsonq.svg) - A simple Go package to Query over JSON Data.
* [gqlgen](https://github.com/99designs/gqlgen) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/99designs/gqlgen.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/99designs/gqlgen.svg) - go generate based graphql server library.
* [graphql](https://github.com/tmc/graphql) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tmc/graphql.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tmc/graphql.svg) - graphql parser + utilities.
* [graphql](https://github.com/neelance/graphql-go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neelance/graphql-go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/neelance/graphql-go.svg) - GraphQL server with a focus on ease of use.
* [graphql-go](https://github.com/graphql-go/graphql) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/graphql-go/graphql.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/graphql-go/graphql.svg) - Implementation of GraphQL for Go.
* [gws](https://github.com/Zaba505/gws) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Zaba505/gws.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Zaba505/gws.svg) - Apollos' "GraphQL over Websocket" client and server implementation.
* [jsonpath](https://github.com/AsaiYusuke/jsonpath) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AsaiYusuke/jsonpath.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AsaiYusuke/jsonpath.svg) - A query library for retrieving part of JSON based on JSONPath syntax.

Filtering, validations, both `AND`, `OR` operations are supported directly in the query.

## Security

*Libraries that are used to help make your application more secure.*

* [acmetool](https://github.com/hlandau/acme) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hlandau/acme.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hlandau/acme.svg) - ACME (Let's Encrypt) client tool with automatic renewal.

* [age](https://github.com/FiloSottile/age) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FiloSottile/age.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FiloSottile/age.svg) - A simple, modern and secure encryption tool (and Go library) with small explicit keys, no config options, and UNIX-style composability. 
* [argon2-hashing](https://github.com/andskur/argon2-hashing) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andskur/argon2-hashing.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/andskur/argon2-hashing.svg) - light wrapper around Go's argon2 package that closely mirrors with Go's standard library Bcrypt and simple-scrypt package.

* [BadActor](https://github.com/jaredfolkins/badactor) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jaredfolkins/badactor.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jaredfolkins/badactor.svg) - In-memory, application-driven jailer built in the spirit of fail2ban.

* [csvutil](https://github.com/jszwec/csvutil) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jszwec/csvutil.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jszwec/csvutil.svg) - High Performance, idiomatic CSV record encoding and decoding to native Go structures.
* [elastic](https://github.com/epiclabs-io/elastic) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/epiclabs-io/elastic.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/epiclabs-io/elastic.svg) - Convert slices, maps or any other unknown value across different types at run-time, no matter what.
* [fixedwidth](https://github.com/huydang284/fixedwidth) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huydang284/fixedwidth.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/huydang284/fixedwidth.svg) - Fixed-width text formatting (UTF-8 supported).
* [fwencoder](https://github.com/o1egl/fwencoder) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/o1egl/fwencoder.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/o1egl/fwencoder.svg) - Fixed width file parser (encoding and decoding library) for Go.
* [go-capnproto](https://github.com/glycerine/go-capnproto) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/glycerine/go-capnproto.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/glycerine/go-capnproto.svg) - Cap'n Proto library and parser for go.
* [go-codec](https://github.com/ugorji/go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ugorji/go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ugorji/go.svg) - High Performance, feature-Rich, idiomatic encode, decode and rpc library for msgpack, cbor and json, with runtime-based OR code-generation support.
* [go-lctree](https://github.com/sbourlon/go-lctree) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sbourlon/go-lctree.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sbourlon/go-lctree.svg) - Provides a CLI and primitives to serialize and deserialize [LeetCode binary trees](https://support.leetcode.com/hc/en-us/articles/360011883654-What-does-1-null-2-3-mean-in-binary-tree-representation).
* [gogoprotobuf](https://github.com/gogo/protobuf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gogo/protobuf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gogo/protobuf.svg) - Protocol Buffers for Go with Gadgets.
* [goprotobuf](https://github.com/golang/protobuf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/protobuf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/protobuf.svg) - Go support, in the form of a library and protocol compiler plugin, for Google's protocol buffers.
* [jsoniter](https://github.com/json-iterator/go) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/json-iterator/go.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/json-iterator/go.svg) - High-performance 100% compatible drop-in replacement of "encoding/json".
* [mapstructure](https://github.com/mitchellh/mapstructure) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mitchellh/mapstructure.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mitchellh/mapstructure.svg) - Go library for decoding generic map values into native Go structures.
* [php_session_decoder](https://github.com/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yvasiyarov/php_session_decoder.svg) - GoLang library for working with PHP session format and PHP Serialize/Unserialize functions.
* [pletter](https://github.com/vimeda/pletter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vimeda/pletter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vimeda/pletter.svg) - A standard way to wrap a proto message for message brokers.
* [structomap](https://github.com/tuvistavie/structomap) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tuvistavie/structomap.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tuvistavie/structomap.svg) - Library to easily and dynamically generate maps from static structures.

## Template Engines

*Libraries and tools for templating and lexing.*

* [ace](https://github.com/yosssi/ace) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yosssi/ace.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yosssi/ace.svg) - Ace is an HTML template engine for Go, inspired by Slim and Jade. Ace is a refinement of Gold.
* [amber](https://github.com/eknkc/amber) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eknkc/amber.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eknkc/amber.svg) - Amber is an elegant templating engine for Go Programming Language It is inspired from HAML and Jade.
* [damsel](https://github.com/dskinner/damsel) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dskinner/damsel.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dskinner/damsel.svg) - Markup language featuring html outlining via css-selectors, extensible via pkg html/template and others.
* [ego](https://github.com/benbjohnson/ego) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benbjohnson/ego.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benbjohnson/ego.svg) - Lightweight templating language that lets you write templates in Go. Templates are translated into Go and compiled.
* [extemplate](https://github.com/dannyvankooten/extemplate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dannyvankooten/extemplate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dannyvankooten/extemplate.svg) - Tiny wrapper around html/template to allow for easy file-based template inheritance.
* [fasttemplate](https://github.com/valyala/fasttemplate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/fasttemplate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/fasttemplate.svg) - Simple and fast template engine. Substitutes template placeholders up to 10x faster than [text/template](https://golang.org/pkg/text/template/).
* [gofpdf](https://github.com/jung-kurt/gofpdf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jung-kurt/gofpdf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jung-kurt/gofpdf.svg) - PDF document generator with high level support for text, drawing and images.
* [gospin](https://github.com/m1/gospin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m1/gospin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/m1/gospin.svg) - Article spinning and spintax/spinning syntax engine, useful for A/B, testing pieces of text/articles and creating more natural conversations.
* [goview](https://github.com/foolin/goview) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/foolin/goview.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/foolin/goview.svg) - Goview is a lightweight, minimalist and idiomatic template library based on golang html/template for building Go web application.
* [hero](https://github.com/shiyanhui/hero) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shiyanhui/hero.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shiyanhui/hero.svg) - Hero is a handy, fast and powerful go template engine.

* [maroto](https://github.com/johnfercher/maroto) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/johnfercher/maroto.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/johnfercher/maroto.svg) - A maroto way to create PDFs. Maroto is inspired in Bootstrap and uses gofpdf. Fast and simple.
* [mustache](https://github.com/hoisie/mustache) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hoisie/mustache.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hoisie/mustache.svg) - Go implementation of the Mustache template language.
* [pongo2](https://github.com/flosch/pongo2) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flosch/pongo2.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/flosch/pongo2.svg) - Django-like template-engine for Go.
* [quicktemplate](https://github.com/valyala/quicktemplate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/quicktemplate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/valyala/quicktemplate.svg) - Fast, powerful, yet easy to use template engine. Converts templates into Go code and then compiles it.
* [raymond](https://github.com/aymerick/raymond) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aymerick/raymond.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aymerick/raymond.svg) - Complete handlebars implementation in Go.

## Testing

*Libraries for testing codebases and generating test data.*

* Testing Frameworks
    * [apitest](https://apitest.dev) - Simple and extensible behavioural testing library for REST based services or HTTP handlers that supports mocking external http calls and rendering of sequence diagrams.
    * [assert](https://github.com/go-playground/assert) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/assert.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/assert.svg) - Basic Assertion Library used along side native go testing, with building blocks for custom assertions.

    * [biff](https://github.com/fulldump/biff) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fulldump/biff.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fulldump/biff.svg) - Bifurcation testing framework, BDD compatible.
    * [charlatan](https://github.com/percolate/charlatan) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/percolate/charlatan.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/percolate/charlatan.svg) - Tool to generate fake interface implementations for tests.

    * [cupaloy](https://github.com/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bradleyjkemp/cupaloy.svg) - Simple snapshot testing addon for your test framework.

    * [ginkgo](https://onsi.github.io/ginkgo/) - BDD Testing Framework for Go.

    * [go-carpet](https://github.com/msoap/go-carpet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/msoap/go-carpet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/msoap/go-carpet.svg) - Tool for viewing test coverage in terminal.

## Text Processing

*Libraries for parsing and manipulating texts.*

* Specific Formats
    * [align](https://github.com/Guitarbum722/align) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Guitarbum722/align.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Guitarbum722/align.svg) - A general purpose application that aligns text.

    * [bbConvert](https://github.com/CalebQ42/bbConvert) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CalebQ42/bbConvert.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CalebQ42/bbConvert.svg) - Converts bbCode to HTML that allows you to add support for custom bbCode tags.

## UUID

*Libraries for working with UUIDs.*

* [goflake](https://github.com/hart87/GoFlake) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hart87/GoFlake.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hart87/GoFlake.svg) - A small, scalable, & serverless unique ID generator for use in distributed systems. Inspired by Twitters Snowflake.
* [goid](https://github.com/jakehl/goid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jakehl/goid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jakehl/goid.svg) - Generate and Parse RFC4122 compliant V4 UUIDs.
* [gouid](https://github.com/twharmon/gouid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/twharmon/gouid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/twharmon/gouid.svg) - Generate cryptographically secure random string IDs with just one allocation.
* [nanoid](https://github.com/aidarkhanov/nanoid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aidarkhanov/nanoid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aidarkhanov/nanoid.svg) - A tiny and efficient Go unique string ID generator.
* [sno](https://github.com/muyo/sno) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muyo/sno.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/muyo/sno.svg) - Compact, sortable and fast unique IDs with embedded metadata.
* [ulid](https://github.com/oklog/ulid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oklog/ulid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oklog/ulid.svg) - Go implementation of ULID (Universally Unique Lexicographically Sortable Identifier).
* [uniq](https://gitlab.com/skilstak/code/go/uniq) - No hassle safe, fast unique identifiers with commands.
* [uuid](https://github.com/agext/uuid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agext/uuid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/agext/uuid.svg) - Generate, encode, and decode UUIDs v1 with fast or cryptographic-quality random node identifier.
* [uuid](https://github.com/gofrs/uuid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gofrs/uuid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gofrs/uuid.svg) - Implementation of Universally Unique Identifier (UUID). Supports both creation and parsing of UUIDs. Actively maintained fork of satori uuid.
* [uuid](https://github.com/google/uuid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/uuid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/google/uuid.svg) - Go package for UUIDs based on RFC 4122 and DCE 1.1: Authentication and Security Services.
* [wuid](https://github.com/edwingeng/wuid) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edwingeng/wuid.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edwingeng/wuid.svg) - An extremely fast unique number generator, 10-135 times faster than UUID.

* [rux](https://github.com/gookit/rux) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gookit/rux.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gookit/rux.svg) - Simple and fast web framework for build golang HTTP applications.
* [tango](https://github.com/lunny/tango) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lunny/tango.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lunny/tango.svg) - Micro & pluggable web framework for Go.
* [tigertonic](https://github.com/rcrowley/go-tigertonic) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rcrowley/go-tigertonic.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rcrowley/go-tigertonic.svg) - Go framework for building JSON web services inspired by Dropwizard.
* [uAdmin](https://github.com/uadmin/uadmin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uadmin/uadmin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uadmin/uadmin.svg) - Fully featured web framework for Golang, inspired by Django.
* [utron](https://github.com/gernest/utron) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gernest/utron.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gernest/utron.svg) - Lightweight MVC framework for Go(Golang).
* [vox](https://github.com/aisk/vox) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aisk/vox.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aisk/vox.svg) - A golang web framework for humans, inspired by Koa heavily.
* [WebGo](https://github.com/bnkamalesh/webgo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bnkamalesh/webgo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bnkamalesh/webgo.svg) - A micro-framework to build web apps; with handler chaining, middleware and context injection. With standard library compliant HTTP handlers(i.e. http.HandlerFunc).
* [YARF](https://github.com/yarf-framework/yarf) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yarf-framework/yarf.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yarf-framework/yarf.svg) - Fast micro-framework designed to build REST APIs and web services in a fast and simple way.

### Middlewares

#### Actual middlewares

* [client-timing](https://github.com/posener/client-timing) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/posener/client-timing.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/posener/client-timing.svg) - An HTTP client for Server-Timing header.
* [CORS](https://github.com/rs/cors) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rs/cors.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rs/cors.svg) - Easily add CORS capabilities to your API.
* [formjson](https://github.com/rs/formjson) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rs/formjson.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rs/formjson.svg) - Transparently handle JSON input as a standard form POST.
* [go-fault](https://github.com/github/go-fault) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/github/go-fault.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/github/go-fault.svg) - Fault injection middleware for Go.
* [go-server-timing](https://github.com/mitchellh/go-server-timing) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mitchellh/go-server-timing.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mitchellh/go-server-timing.svg) - Add/parse Server-Timing header.
* [Limiter](https://github.com/ulule/limiter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ulule/limiter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ulule/limiter.svg) - Dead simple rate limit middleware for Go.
* [ln-paywall](https://github.com/philippgille/ln-paywall) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/philippgille/ln-paywall.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/philippgille/ln-paywall.svg) - Go middleware for monetizing APIs on a per-request basis with the Lightning Network (Bitcoin).
* [rk-gin](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-gin) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rookie-ninja/rk-gin.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rookie-ninja/rk-gin.svg) - Middleware for Gin framework with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
* [rk-grpc](https://github.com/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rookie-ninja/rk-grpc.svg) - Middleware for gRPC with logging, metrics, auth, tracing etc.
* [Tollbooth](https://github.com/didip/tollbooth) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/didip/tollbooth.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/didip/tollbooth.svg) - Rate limit HTTP request handler.
* [XFF](https://github.com/sebest/xff) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sebest/xff.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sebest/xff.svg) - Handle `X-Forwarded-For` header and friends.

#### Libraries for creating HTTP middlewares

* [alice](https://github.com/justinas/alice) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/justinas/alice.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/justinas/alice.svg) - Painless middleware chaining for Go.
* [catena](https://github.com/codemodus/catena) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codemodus/catena.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codemodus/catena.svg) - http.Handler wrapper catenation (same API as "chain").
* [chain](https://github.com/codemodus/chain) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codemodus/chain.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codemodus/chain.svg) - Handler wrapper chaining with scoped data (net/context-based "middleware").
* [go-wrap](https://github.com/go-on/wrap) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-on/wrap.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-on/wrap.svg) - Small middlewares package for net/http.
* [gores](https://github.com/alioygur/gores) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alioygur/gores.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alioygur/gores.svg) - Go package that handles HTML, JSON, XML and etc. responses. Useful for RESTful APIs.
* [interpose](https://github.com/carbocation/interpose) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carbocation/interpose.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/carbocation/interpose.svg) - Minimalist net/http middleware for golang.
* [mediary](https://github.com/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HereMobilityDevelopers/mediary.svg) - add interceptors to `http.Client` to allow dumping/shaping/tracing/... of requests/responses.
* [muxchain](https://github.com/stephens2424/muxchain) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stephens2424/muxchain.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stephens2424/muxchain.svg) - Lightweight middleware for net/http.
* [negroni](https://github.com/urfave/negroni) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/urfave/negroni.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/urfave/negroni.svg) - Idiomatic HTTP middleware for Golang.
* [render](https://github.com/unrolled/render) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/unrolled/render.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/unrolled/render.svg) - Go package for easily rendering JSON, XML, and HTML template responses.
* [renderer](https://github.com/thedevsaddam/renderer) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thedevsaddam/renderer.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thedevsaddam/renderer.svg) - Simple, lightweight and faster response (JSON, JSONP, XML, YAML, HTML, File) rendering package for Go.
* [rye](https://github.com/InVisionApp/rye) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/InVisionApp/rye.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/InVisionApp/rye.svg) - Tiny Go middleware library (with canned Middlewares) that supports JWT, CORS, Statsd, and Go 1.7 context.
* [stats](https://github.com/thoas/stats) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thoas/stats.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thoas/stats.svg) - Go middleware that stores various information about your web application.

### Routers

* [alien](https://github.com/gernest/alien) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gernest/alien.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gernest/alien.svg) - Lightweight and fast http router from outer space.
* [bellt](https://github.com/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/GuilhermeCaruso/bellt.svg) - A simple Go HTTP router.
* [Bone](https://github.com/go-zoo/bone) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-zoo/bone.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-zoo/bone.svg) - Lightning Fast HTTP Multiplexer.
* [Bxog](https://github.com/claygod/Bxog) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/claygod/Bxog.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/claygod/Bxog.svg) - Simple and fast HTTP router for Go. It works with routes of varying difficulty, length and nesting. And he knows how to create a URL from the received parameters.
* [chi](https://github.com/go-chi/chi) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-chi/chi.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-chi/chi.svg) - Small, fast and expressive HTTP router built on net/context.
* [fasthttprouter](https://github.com/buaazp/fasthttprouter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/buaazp/fasthttprouter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/buaazp/fasthttprouter.svg) - High performance router forked from `httprouter`. The first router fit for `fasthttp`.
* [FastRouter](https://github.com/razonyang/fastrouter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/razonyang/fastrouter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/razonyang/fastrouter.svg) - a fast, flexible HTTP router written in Go.
* [gocraft/web](https://github.com/gocraft/web) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gocraft/web.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gocraft/web.svg) - Mux and middleware package in Go.
* [Goji](https://github.com/goji/goji) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/goji/goji.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/goji/goji.svg) - Goji is a minimalistic and flexible HTTP request multiplexer with support for `net/context`.
* [goroute](https://github.com/goroute/route) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/goroute/route.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/goroute/route.svg) - Simple yet powerful HTTP request multiplexer.
* [GoRouter](https://github.com/vardius/gorouter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vardius/gorouter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vardius/gorouter.svg) - GoRouter is a Server/API micro framework, HTTP request router, multiplexer, mux that provides request router with middleware supporting `net/context`.
* [gowww/router](https://github.com/gowww/router) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gowww/router.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gowww/router.svg) - Lightning fast HTTP router fully compatible with the net/http.Handler interface.
* [httprouter](https://github.com/julienschmidt/httprouter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/julienschmidt/httprouter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/julienschmidt/httprouter.svg) - High performance router. Use this and the standard http handlers to form a very high performance web framework.
* [httptreemux](https://github.com/dimfeld/httptreemux) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dimfeld/httptreemux.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dimfeld/httptreemux.svg) - High-speed, flexible tree-based HTTP router for Go. Inspiration from httprouter.
* [lars](https://github.com/go-playground/lars) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/lars.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/lars.svg) - Is a lightweight, fast and extensible zero allocation HTTP router for Go used to create customizable frameworks.
* [mux](https://github.com/gorilla/mux) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gorilla/mux.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gorilla/mux.svg) - Powerful URL router and dispatcher for golang.
* [ozzo-routing](https://github.com/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-ozzo/ozzo-routing.svg) - An extremely fast Go (golang) HTTP router that supports regular expression route matching. Comes with full support for building RESTful APIs.
* [pure](https://github.com/go-playground/pure) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/pure.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-playground/pure.svg) - Is a lightweight HTTP router that sticks to the std "net/http" implementation.
* [Siesta](https://github.com/VividCortex/siesta) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VividCortex/siesta.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/VividCortex/siesta.svg) - Composable framework to write middleware and handlers.
* [vestigo](https://github.com/husobee/vestigo) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/husobee/vestigo.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/husobee/vestigo.svg) - Performant, stand-alone, HTTP compliant URL Router for go web applications.
* [violetear](https://github.com/nbari/violetear) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nbari/violetear.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nbari/violetear.svg) - Go HTTP router.
* [xmux](https://github.com/rs/xmux) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rs/xmux.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rs/xmux.svg) - High performance muxer based on `httprouter` with `net/context` support.
* [xujiajun/gorouter](https://github.com/xujiajun/gorouter) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xujiajun/gorouter.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xujiajun/gorouter.svg) - A simple and fast HTTP router for Go.

## XML

* [XML-Comp](https://github.com/xml-comp/xml-comp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xml-comp/xml-comp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xml-comp/xml-comp.svg) - Simple command line XML comparer that generates diffs of folders, files and tags.

# Tools

*Go software and plugins.*

**[⬆ back to top](#contents)**

## Code Analysis

* [apicompat](https://github.com/bradleyfalzon/apicompat) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bradleyfalzon/apicompat.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bradleyfalzon/apicompat.svg) - Checks recent changes to a Go project for backwards incompatible changes.
* [dupl](https://github.com/mibk/dupl) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mibk/dupl.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mibk/dupl.svg) - Tool for code clone detection.
* [errcheck](https://github.com/kisielk/errcheck) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kisielk/errcheck.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kisielk/errcheck.svg) - Errcheck is a program for checking for unchecked errors in Go programs.
* [gcvis](https://github.com/davecheney/gcvis) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davecheney/gcvis.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davecheney/gcvis.svg) - Visualise Go program GC trace data in real time.
* [go-checkstyle](https://github.com/qiniu/checkstyle) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qiniu/checkstyle.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/qiniu/checkstyle.svg) - checkstyle is a style check tool like java checkstyle. This tool inspired by java checkstyle, golint. The style referred to some points in Go Code Review Comments.
* [go-cleanarch](https://github.com/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/roblaszczak/go-cleanarch.svg) - go-cleanarch was created to validate Clean Architecture rules, like a The Dependency Rule and interaction between packages in your Go projects.
* [go-critic](https://github.com/go-critic/go-critic) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-critic/go-critic.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/go-critic/go-critic.svg) - source code linter that brings checks that are currently not implemented in other linters.
* [go-mod-outdated](https://github.com/psampaz/go-mod-outdated) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/psampaz/go-mod-outdated.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/psampaz/go-mod-outdated.svg) - An easy way to find outdated dependencies of your Go projects.
* [go-outdated](https://github.com/firstrow/go-outdated) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/firstrow/go-outdated.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/firstrow/go-outdated.svg) - Console application that displays outdated packages.
* [goast-viewer](https://github.com/yuroyoro/goast-viewer) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yuroyoro/goast-viewer.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yuroyoro/goast-viewer.svg) - Web based Golang AST visualizer.
* [GoCover.io](https://gocover.io/) - GoCover.io offers the code coverage of any golang package as a service.
* [goimports](https://godoc.org/golang.org/x/tools/cmd/goimports) - Tool to fix (add, remove) your Go imports automatically.
* [golang-ifood-sdk](https://github.com/arxdsilva/golang-ifood-sdk) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arxdsilva/golang-ifood-sdk.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arxdsilva/golang-ifood-sdk.svg) - iFood API SDK.
* [golines](https://github.com/segmentio/golines) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/segmentio/golines.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/segmentio/golines.svg) - Formatter that automatically shortens long lines in Go code.
* [GoLint](https://github.com/golang/lint) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/lint.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/golang/lint.svg) - Golint is a linter for Go source code.
* [Golint online](http://go-lint.appspot.com/) - Lints online Go source files on GitHub, Bitbucket and Google Project Hosting using the golint package.
* [GoPlantUML](https://github.com/jfeliu007/goplantuml) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jfeliu007/goplantuml.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jfeliu007/goplantuml.svg) - Library and CLI that generates text plantump class diagram containing information about structures and interfaces with the relationship among them.
* [goreturns](https://sourcegraph.com/github.com/sqs/goreturns) - Adds zero-value return statements to match the func return types.
* [gosimple](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/gosimple) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dominikh/go-tools.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dominikh/go-tools.svg) - gosimple is a linter for Go source code that specialises on simplifying code.
* [gostatus](https://github.com/shurcooL/gostatus) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shurcooL/gostatus.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shurcooL/gostatus.svg) - Command line tool, shows the status of repositories that contain Go packages.
* [lint](https://github.com/surullabs/lint) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/surullabs/lint.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/surullabs/lint.svg) - Run linters as part of go test.
* [php-parser](https://github.com/z7zmey/php-parser) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/z7zmey/php-parser.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/z7zmey/php-parser.svg) - A Parser for PHP written in Go.
* [staticcheck](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/staticcheck) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dominikh/go-tools.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dominikh/go-tools.svg) - staticcheck is `go vet` on steroids, applying a ton of static analysis checks you might be used to from tools like ReSharper for C#.
* [tarp](https://github.com/verygoodsoftwarenotvirus/tarp) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/verygoodsoftwarenotvirus/tarp.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/verygoodsoftwarenotvirus/tarp.svg) - tarp finds functions and methods without direct unit tests in Go source code.
* [tickgit](https://github.com/augmentable-dev/tickgit) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/augmentable-dev/tickgit.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/augmentable-dev/tickgit.svg) - CLI and go package for surfacing code comment TODOs (in any language) and applying a `git blame`to identify the author.
* [unconvert](https://github.com/mdempsky/unconvert) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdempsky/unconvert.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mdempsky/unconvert.svg) - Remove unnecessary type conversions from Go source.
* [unused](https://github.com/dominikh/go-tools/tree/master/cmd/unused) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dominikh/go-tools.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dominikh/go-tools.svg) - unused checks Go code for unused constants, variables, functions and types.
* [validate](https://github.com/mccoyst/validate) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mccoyst/validate.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mccoyst/validate.svg) - Automatically validates struct fields with tags.

* [lstags](https://github.com/ivanilves/lstags) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivanilves/lstags.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ivanilves/lstags.svg) - Tool and API to sync Docker images across different registries.
* [lwc](https://github.com/timdp/lwc) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/timdp/lwc.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/timdp/lwc.svg) - A live-updating version of the UNIX wc command.
* [manssh](https://github.com/xwjdsh/manssh) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xwjdsh/manssh.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xwjdsh/manssh.svg) - manssh is a command line tool for managing your ssh alias config easily.
* [Moby](https://github.com/moby/moby) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/moby/moby.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/moby/moby.svg) - Collaborative project for the container ecosystem to assemble container-based systems.
* [Mora](https://github.com/emicklei/mora) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emicklei/mora.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emicklei/mora.svg) - REST server for accessing MongoDB documents and meta data.
* [ostent](https://github.com/ostrost/ostent) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ostrost/ostent.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ostrost/ostent.svg) - collects and displays system metrics and optionally relays to Graphite and/or InfluxDB.
* [Packer](https://github.com/mitchellh/packer) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mitchellh/packer.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mitchellh/packer.svg) - Packer is a tool for creating identical machine images for multiple platforms from a single source configuration.
* [Pewpew](https://github.com/bengadbois/pewpew) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bengadbois/pewpew.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bengadbois/pewpew.svg) - Flexible HTTP command line stress tester.

* [Rodent](https://github.com/alouche/rodent) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alouche/rodent.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alouche/rodent.svg) - Rodent helps you manage Go versions, projects and track dependencies.

* [sg](https://github.com/ChristopherRabotin/sg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChristopherRabotin/sg.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ChristopherRabotin/sg.svg) - Benchmarks a set of HTTP endpoints (like ab), with possibility to use the response code and data between each call for specific server stress based on its previous response.

## Benchmarks

* [autobench](https://github.com/davecheney/autobench) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davecheney/autobench.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davecheney/autobench.svg) - Framework to compare the performance between different Go versions.
* [go-benchmark-app](https://github.com/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrLSD/go-benchmark-app.svg) - Powerful HTTP-benchmark tool mixed with Аb, Wrk, Siege tools. Gathering statistics and various parameters for benchmarks and comparison results.
* [go-benchmarks](https://github.com/tylertreat/go-benchmarks) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tylertreat/go-benchmarks.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tylertreat/go-benchmarks.svg) - Few miscellaneous Go microbenchmarks. Compare some language features to alternative approaches.
* [go-http-routing-benchmark](https://github.com/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/julienschmidt/go-http-routing-benchmark.svg) - Go HTTP request router benchmark and comparison.
* [go-json-benchmark](https://github.com/zerosnake0/go-json-benchmark) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zerosnake0/go-json-benchmark.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zerosnake0/go-json-benchmark.svg) - Go JSON benchmark.
* [go-ml-benchmarks](https://github.com/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nikolaydubina/go-ml-benchmarks.svg) - benchmarks for machine learning inference in Go.
* [go-web-framework-benchmark](https://github.com/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smallnest/go-web-framework-benchmark.svg) - Go web framework benchmark.
* [go_serialization_benchmarks](https://github.com/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alecthomas/go_serialization_benchmarks.svg) - Benchmarks of Go serialization methods.
* [gocostmodel](https://github.com/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PuerkitoBio/gocostmodel.svg) - Benchmarks of common basic operations for the Go language.
* [golang-sql-benchmark](https://github.com/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tyler-smith/golang-sql-benchmark.svg) - Collection of benchmarks for popular Go database/SQL utilities.
* [gospeed](https://github.com/feyeleanor/GoSpeed) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/feyeleanor/GoSpeed.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/feyeleanor/GoSpeed.svg) - Go micro-benchmarks for calculating the speed of language constructs.
* [kvbench](https://github.com/jimrobinson/kvbench) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jimrobinson/kvbench.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jimrobinson/kvbench.svg) - Key/Value database benchmark.
* [skynet](https://github.com/atemerev/skynet) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/atemerev/skynet.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/atemerev/skynet.svg) - Skynet 1M threads microbenchmark.
* [speedtest-resize](https://github.com/fawick/speedtest-resize) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fawick/speedtest-resize.svg) ![stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fawick/speedtest-resize.svg) - Compare various Image resize algorithms for the Go language.
